Smuggling Contraband and Silver: Relics of Shanhaiguan; Ancestral Temple of Smuggling; Japanese Authorities Use the Surplus to Build Elementary School; Teaching Japanese Children and Serving as Japanese Association 80

A Shanhaiguan correspondent of the Mainland Daily News reported on the 4th that smuggling from Shanhaiguan by land to Qinhuangdao has been sporadic for the past six weeks. A few days ago, it suddenly stopped completely and switched to sea routes. However, the relics of smuggling will remain here for a long time and cannot be destroyed without earthquakes or other disasters. The Japanese authorities in Shanhaiguan used the surplus profits from smuggling to build a magnificent three-story elementary school to teach the children of Japanese residents in Shanhaiguan. Its address is adjacent to the Chinese customs. Apart from the buildings of the "Manchukuo" customs and post office, its architecture can be called the most magnificent here. If there is an ancestral master of smuggling in the world, then this building can be named "Ancestral Temple of Smuggling." In addition to serving as a school for Japanese children, the building also serves as a meeting place for Japanese residents. These people gather in it from time to time to discuss. Inquiring with customs personnel and others, I carefully inquired about the origin of the establishment of the building. It is said that when silver smuggling was at its peak in the summer of 1935, the customs anti-smuggling team encountered various difficulties. More than 400,000 silver dollars were smuggled through Shanhaiguan every day. Each train was full of Koreans smuggling silver when it arrived from Tianjin. After the customs seized it, it was confiscated. However, very few were found. Most of them crossed the Great Wall and entered the territory of "Manchukuo." The customs repeatedly asked the Japanese police and the Japanese military authorities to assist in the arrest, but the effectiveness was minimal. Before long, the customs anti-smuggling team was forced to be unable to patrol on the Great Wall. The smugglers mostly threw the silver into "Manchukuo" from the top of the Great Wall. Two smugglers, one Manchu and one Japanese, fell to the ground from the city and died. Therefore, the Japanese military authorities prevented the customs anti-smuggling team from patrolling on the city. As a result, the smugglers became more unscrupulous, and the number seized by the customs decreased day by day. Not long after, the police of the Japanese consulate suddenly began to search for silver smuggled by Koreans. The customs authorities were surprised, and the elementary school building began to be built at this time. Later, it was learned that the construction cost was all derived from the surplus profits of silver. The Japanese police exchanged the silver dollars seized from the Koreans for paper money, but did not send it to the Chinese customs. The exchange shops in the pseudo-Manchu territory outside the Great Wall, which were often taken care of by smugglers, sold the silver dollars at market prices. The remaining profits were accumulated to pay for the construction of the elementary school. Then the Japanese police suddenly stopped searching for silver, because the elementary school building had been completed.

Siberian Railway Almost Exclusively Used for Soviet Military Purposes: Summary of Japanese Spy Report; Attacking Soviet Russia for Disrupting Peace 81

Harbin Correspondence: The Japanese-Russian War is being planned in the open or prepared in secret every day. Currently, the Japanese side is using the strategy of controlling Inner Mongolia, encircling Outer Mongolia, and attacking the Soviet Union. The Soviet Union is actively responding to the war and views the Japanese side as even more aggressive. Both sides send many spies to probe military actions, and they are active everywhere. According to a report from a Japanese spy to the military, the Soviet Union is mobilizing military trains on the Siberian Railway extremely frequently, so that international express trains must give way. For example, an international train once stopped at Oyahee Station for as long as fourteen hours, allowing twenty-eight Soviet military trains to pass before the international train could depart. Also, in the station premises of Novosibirsk, there were three trains fully loaded with 150 military trucks each, and two trains fully loaded with 200 military trucks each. At Daria Station, there were three trains carrying tanks, one of which had twenty large tanks, and the other two had thirty small tanks each. Regarding the Soviet Union's expansion of its Far East military preparations, the Japanese side, based on this information, launched a large-scale attack and propaganda, believing that the Soviet Union was disrupting peace in the Far East. However, the Japanese themselves do not practice what they preach. I don't know how they can justify themselves.

All the work of the Hebei-Chahar Political Affairs Committee is proceeding as usual, but there is no special progress. In order to maintain the security of Beijing and prevent unscrupulous people from taking the opportunity to make trouble, the authorities send troops to guard the city walls every night and patrol. Since its implementation, it has been quite effective. However, as for the opium poppy seeds in the various counties, in addition to the seeds in the counties that have already been banned in the first phase, which have already been destroyed, although the various counties that are banned in the second phase are being investigated, it is feared that the people do not understand the great righteousness and still secretly store the seeds, hoping to secretly plant them. They should all be destroyed in order to fundamentally eliminate them. An order has now been issued to the various counties that are banning opium planting in the second phase and to the prohibition commissioners to supervise and destroy all the opium poppy seeds in the counties and report the compliance situation for inspection.

Robbing Groups in Xingning: Natural Disasters and Famine; People Have No Food 84

In addition, rumors are rampant, legal tender is falling in price, and foreign rice is soaring, with a price of 13 yuan per 100 catties. Leading people in Xingning County, therefore, set out to rob food. In Yangziling, Shima, Fengshu, Huangjingtang, Yanggangtou, Yandun, Gantang, Liantangli, and other places in Longtian District, there are cries of distress everywhere. Hunger-stricken people set out in teams every day, each team of more than 200 people, dressed in rags, emaciated, and looking like they are starving, going to homes that are slightly better off to make a fuss about the famine. They bring men, women, and children, crying miserably. Their whereabouts are uncertain every day. If they encounter a long journey, they will camp in the wilderness. Currently, the poor people of all ethnic groups in the county have no way to survive and are rioting everywhere to prolong their lives. They have convened the elders of each ethnic group to discuss relief in order to appease the poor. For example, the Zhang Ethnic Self-Government Association, after preparations were completed, planned to provide relief. First, investigation forms were issued to investigate the names, genders, ages, village names, and house names of the heads of households to be relieved. After the investigation is completed, relief will be provided according to the list. The Chen ethnic elders of Dongshan Temple in Nipi District also planned to raise funds from various ancestral temples and wealthy people to provide relief for one month. The Pan ethnic elders of Dachiwu in Yonghe District specially persuaded the wealthy fathers to donate, raising more than 1,000 yuan and dozens of stones of white rice, planning to provide relief during the day. The headquarters of the Third Army Seventh Division stationed there also allocated 1,000 yuan to the relief association to provide relief to the hungry people. In order to provide relief to the hungry people by providing work, the headquarters issued a notice recruiting 600 workers to repair the collapsed river embankments. After the completion, it was changed to a provincial highway protection team, with a monthly salary of 15 yuan (including food), which was issued by the division. Now that the poor people have heard the news, they are flocking to the department to be hired. (4th)

Songjiang: Section Chief Publicly Admits Fault 85

The fourth phase of reissuing opium addiction cessation licenses in this county has long expired, but there are still many omissions. The county government dispatched officials to the districts along with County Magistrate Li to supervise the replacement. Yesterday, the First District Office specially convened an emergency meeting of all township chiefs. Feng Gengbai, the section chief of the Fourth Section of the county government, and He Runzhang, the director of the Public Security Bureau, attended. The township chiefs of the district, led by Ding Shilong, the chief of Piyun Town, worked hard to handle the self-renewal registration, and were ordered to commend them. However, on the one hand, they aroused the resentment of opium addicts, and then suffered the slander of villains, and presented a complaint to the provincial authorities. [Illegible] The county magistrate received training and went to Beijing, and approved "Inquire and verify." The section chief in charge, without the consent of the acting county magistrate Secretary Shen, [illegible] conducted a trial by a forwarding trial officer, interrogated and sent him to jail. The township chiefs felt that there was no guarantee in handling opium prohibition, and they resigned collectively on the spot. Then Director He earnestly explained, and Section Chief Feng realized his mistake and publicly admitted his fault. After District Chief Shen comforted them, they cancelled their resignations.

Suzhou: Continuing Disturbance of Farmers in Xietang Township 86

In Xietang, Suzhou, there have been waves of rent resistance since last year. At noon on the 8th, 400 to 500 villagers from Xialian Village in the area went to Yuxiang nearby and completely destroyed the houses of seven families, including Baolong Li Jinliang, Li Jiaquan, Zhang Defu, Zhang Hongqi, Zhang Shaoxiang, Zhang Muxiang, and Zhang Rongru. The Security Team stationed in Xietang rushed to the scene after hearing the news. The villagers who caused the trouble had already dispersed, leaving only three people, including the old woman Li Shenshi. The team was taken away, and that night, they were bailed out by the Baozhang and others. However, at about 5 pm, a village child, 5 years old, drowned in the river two miles away from Yuxiang. The villagers of Xialian falsely accused the child of being drowned by the Security Team. At about 6 am on the 9th, more than 300 people gathered again and went to the Xietang Town Security Branch to negotiate, and clashed with the guards of the Security Team, and grabbed firearms. The guards were outnumbered and were rushed into the second gate. The Security Team had no choice but to fire thirty or forty shots into the air, and the villagers temporarily retreated. Currently, this disturbance has not been resolved. The drowned child has been reported to the local court for an autopsy.

Robbery Near [Illegible] Gate 87

The Lu family in Gaojiajiao, south of Huoshaoqiao, four miles away from [Illegible] Gate, was suddenly attacked by more than 40 bandits at about 11 pm the night before last. First, the victim was tied up and beaten. As a result, clothing, jewelry, legal tender, and cash totaling more than 1,000 yuan were robbed. The police station in charge ordered all the police to set out at about 1 am yesterday morning to the scene of the incident to strictly apprehend the bandits.

Wuxi: A Collection of Information Regarding the Silk Cocoon Market 88

Since the opening of the weighing scales at the silk cocoon merchants in Xiyi, yesterday marked the fourth day. Here is a record of various pieces of information:

Previously, the County Agricultural Association, due to the Silk Cocoon Guild setting the cocoon prices too low, had submitted a request to the County Party Headquarters and the County Government to jointly consult with Zeng Jikuan, the director of the Jiangsu Sericulture Management Improvement Committee, inviting leaders of the silk cocoon industry to negotiate and agree to raise the cocoon price. The opening price was set at 32 yuan as the standard. Recently, they received an approval order from the Ministry of Industry, and have already sent a letter to the National Economic Committee's Sericulture Improvement Association to investigate and handle the matter accordingly. In addition, the Jiangsu Construction Department has also sent a telegram instructing the Sericulture Model District to investigate the recent silk prices and silkworm rearing costs, and to negotiate with the Silk Cocoon Guild to handle the matter properly.

The County Magistrate of Long County, considering the current cocoon market and the importance of maintaining security, has implemented very thorough preventative measures. However, on the first day of the opening of the scales, a robbery occurred at the Yuanju Silk Cocoon Merchant, with stolen cocoons amounting to over 6,000 yuan. Recognizing the significant relationship between this incident and the cocoon market, the County Magistrate has specifically convened all county public security, land and water police officers for an important meeting this morning to ensure strict prevention.

The rural silk cocoon merchants are experiencing a surge in shipments, and the quality of the cocoons is good. The highest cocoon price is 38 yuan, with the reeling price at 34 yuan.

According to reports from neighboring counties by the Silk Cocoon Guild, the highest price in Jiangyin is 45 yuan, with the reeling price at 41 yuan, and shipments are still strong. Liyang has a large volume of shipments, and the quality of the cocoons is good, with a reeling price of 29 yuan. Wujin has cocoons of excellent quality, with a high estimated price of 36 yuan and a reeling price of 32 yuan.

With the arrival of new cocoons on the market, various silk mills are also successively starting their machinery. As of yesterday, 37 mills have already started, and several others, including the Luoshe Weixin Mill, are also preparing to start their machinery.

The Sericulture Model District, with the spring cocoons already on the market and the autumn silkworm egg ordering about to begin, and considering that the required quantities by silkworm farmers and merchants in various regions often result in surpluses or shortages, has specifically established a method: those requiring silkworm eggs should first place orders with the egg production farms in their respective districts by July 10th.

Tan Jiujin's Arrest and Transfer to Wuxi 89

Xu Dafu and others, residents of Shazhou Town, the seventh district of Changshu, obstructed river construction. The County Security Team dispatched personnel to the villages and arrested 14 people, including Xu Dafu and Ding Shishu, and transferred them to the Wuxi District Security Command for interrogation. Subsequently, the Provincial Government investigated and determined that the case fell under the scope of ordinary criminal matters and did not require military law processing. It ordered the Changshu County Government to send police officers to Wuxi to present a report to District Commander Zang Qifang, who then transferred Xu Dafu and the other 13 individuals back to Changshu. The main culprit in the case, Tan Jiujin, remained at large. Commissioner Zang ordered all counties to investigate and apprehend him. Yesterday, Dai Shouquan, a detective from the Wuxi County Public Security Bureau, arrested Tan in Changshu and escorted him to Wuxi for transfer to the Commissioner's Office for interrogation. Furthermore, based on a confidential report, the Commissioner's Office learned that Hu Derong and Qin Yunsheng, residents of the Jiaochang area in Changshu, were selling illicit opium. The Commissioner secretly ordered the Changshu County Government to arrest Hu and Qin and to confiscate half a catty of opium, all of which were to be transferred to the Commissioner's Office in Wuxi for legal proceedings.

Striving for Exemption from Stamp Duty 90

The Jiangsu Provincial Federation of Commerce, because the Ministry of Finance required that receipts for membership fees collected by various trade associations be subject to stamp duty according to the rate schedule in Article 16 of the Stamp Tax Law, Section 2, for receipts of money, goods, and materials, decided at a joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees to send a telegram to the Ministry of Finance to strongly advocate for exemption.

The Ministry of Finance issued a reply, stating: "Upon investigation, this matter was also reported to the Ministry by the Beiping Municipal Chamber of Commerce via telegram. The item of 'receipts of money' requires that, with the exception of those issued by government agencies, all individuals or organizations, regardless of whether they are individuals or groups, should pay stamp duty according to the law, and there is no provision for exemption for those not containing business characteristics. Trade associations are not government agencies, so their receipts for collecting membership fees cannot be an exception. As for the item of account books, according to the Stamp Tax Law, it is limited to those used for business purposes. Individuals and educational, cultural, and charitable organizations do not have business characteristics, so their account books should be exempt from stamp duty. However, receipts for money should still be stamped as required. The original report's claims are also a misunderstanding. The request to exempt receipts for membership fees collected by public associations from stamp duty should not be considered." Yesterday, the Federation of Commerce sent letters to the chambers of commerce in various counties for their information.

Changshu: Prison Warden Extorts Inmates 91

The opium offender Wang Baiying was previously sentenced and sent to prison. The prison warden, Tong Guangquan, discovered that Wang's family had a , and extorted a customary fee of 200 yuan. Unexpectedly, the Wang family's had already closed down and could not afford to pay. Tong then instructed veteran inmates to inflict various kinds of abusive practices and beatings on Wang. When the county magistrate went to the prison to promote anti-opium awareness, Wang informed him of this matter. The county magistrate severely reprimanded the warden and others. However, after the county magistrate left, Tong became even more enraged and ordered the beatings to continue, using large iron chains to add to the punishment. Wang's wife, Weng, learned of this and specifically filed a complaint with the county government, requesting a thorough investigation to redress the injustice.

Haimen: Scheduled Joint Examination for Elementary School Students 92

The Education Bureau held a committee meeting yesterday to decide on the joint graduation examination for all elementary schools in the county. It was decided that the examination would be held on the 21st of this month at three locations: the first location is Zhongshan Hall, designated for students from Central Elementary School and eight other schools; the second location is Qilin School, designated for students from Qilin Elementary School and seven other schools; the third location is Haixia School, and it was decided to hold it on the 28th of this month. All collaborative groups were notified to handle the matter through the chief school.

Jiangyin: Spring Cocoon Merchants Open Scales Simultaneously 93

All 32 silk cocoon merchants in the county opened their scales simultaneously on the 7th, in accordance with a resolution from a public meeting. The standard cocoon prices are 20 yuan for improved varieties and 20 yuan for native varieties. After the opening of the scales, some merchants collected as many as 40 to 50 dan, while others collected as few as 10 dan. The highest reeling price was at Dachang in Zhouzhuang, at 41 yuan, while the lowest was at Hantonglong in Shanzhengqiao, at 25 yuan per dan. The cocoon market harvest is still good, and it is expected that goods will flood in after four or five days.

Haizhou: Daughter Kills Father for Money 94

In Longju Town, the second district of this county, there was an elderly resident named Zhang, over sixty years old. One day, he went to the market to sell an ox for forty yuan. On his way back, as it was getting dark, he took a detour to his married daughter's home. After dinner, the daughter saw the money he was carrying and immediately asked her father for a loan. The old man refused. Late at night, the daughter, driven by greed, took advantage of her father's deep sleep and used a knife to kill him. She hid the body under the bed. The next day, the old man's wife and son noticed that he had not arrived at their home. Later, they accidentally discovered the body under the bed, and the crime was exposed. The old man's wife and children immediately handed the daughter over to the nearby military unit and requested that she be sent to the county government for legal proceedings.

Yangzhou: Organizing a Riverbank Protection Association 95

Due to the river's turbulent flow and the increasing erosion of the riverbanks along the river, Zhu Zhuxuan and others convened a meeting of various circles at the County Chamber of Commerce at 3 PM on the 8th to discuss relief measures. It was decided to organize the Jiangdu County Riverbank Protection Preparatory Committee, and Zhu Zhuxuan, Hong Keting, Fu Shaoliu, Zhu Ganchen, Zhang Shaoqi, Dai Xingyi, Yi Liu, Hu Bailing, Bao Xiangzhong, Zhang Jichuan, Liu Boshu, Zhong Xinfu, and Liu Xiaodong were elected as the 13 members of the preparatory committee. The committee's address is temporarily set at the County Chamber of Commerce, and after inviting fellow villagers traveling in Beijing and other provinces to join the organization, a formal meeting will be held.

Luhe: Rewarding and Punishing Anti-Opium Personnel 96

This county has been quite serious about handling anti-opium matters this time. The entire town is divided into seven districts. Although the district chiefs have worked hard on matters such as the self-registration of opium users, the investigation and crackdown on opium users, and the general reporting of opium offenders, their results have been ordinary. However, the first district chief, Chen Weifen, and the seventh district chief, Zhu Qishou, have been extremely diligent in their work and have been commended by the Provincial Department of Civil Affairs. County Magistrate Qi Yunlong has also worked extremely hard on anti-opium matters, and the Provincial Department has not only compiled the case for handling but also issued a strict warning to Xia Yuanzheng, the director of the county's drug rehabilitation center, for incomplete facilities and lack of results, in order to show punishment.

Hangzhou: Execution of Bandit 97

Jin Quanshui, a notorious bandit from Sheng County, also known as Quanshui Mapi, repeatedly committed robbery, murder, kidnapping, and extortion with his gang, including Zhou Rongting, in the county. The authorities strictly pursued them, but they hid in Shanghai. Recently, detectives from the Security Office captured him and escorted him to Hangzhou. After interrogation and confirmation, he was sentenced to death. At 9 AM on the 9th, the bandit was taken from the military prison and escorted to Qingtai Gate for execution by firing squad. The bandit was about fifty years old. He smoked and drank alcohol before the execution, maintaining a natural demeanor. Seven other bandits captured at the same time, including Shen Changqing, will be dealt with in separate cases.

The total cost is 500,000 yuan, invested by the China Farmers Bank, and will cooperate with the Department of Civil Affairs to complete the warehouse network in each county, so that agricultural products can be stored, and banks can easily carry out warehouse mortgage loans, circulating rural finance.

The Yinxian District Administrative Commissioner's Office and the District Security Command received instructions from the Zhejiang Provincial Government that Yinxian, being located near the East China Sea and being a key area in the East China Sea, must actively carry out air defense drill preparations and complete them before the end of June, with drills to be held in July. It is understood that after receiving the order, the Commissioner's Office has sent letters to political parties, government agencies, groups, and schools, and has scheduled a meeting for 2 PM on June 10th to discuss the implementation plan.

Yao Salt Merchants Go to the Province to Petition 101

Since the Yaochang light tax salt price was agreed upon by both parties and the Transportation Office instructed the left field director to comply, each kiln could have collected salt and paid funds earlier. Unexpectedly, all the boatmen and a small number of kiln merchants believed that the new system, once implemented, would be quite detrimental, so they were passive and refused to comply, attempting to overturn the new system. Although the salt merchants petitioned several times, it was not implemented. The salt merchants believed that there was no prospect of collecting salt and that their livelihoods were in jeopardy. Yesterday, they united the salt merchants from the seven districts and held a meeting in Andong, deciding to send Wang Xizheng and four others to the province to petition the Transportation Office, demanding that salt be collected and funds be paid as soon as possible to alleviate the people's hardship.

A Large Number of Bandits Executed by Firing Squad 102

The Yinxian District Security Command, under orders, executed six bandits by firing squad at Caoma Road at approximately 3 PM on the 6th. These bandits, Wang Erde, Wu Asan, Li Yichuan, Chen Amei, Xiang Huageng, and Yang Afu, had repeatedly committed robberies in the Yinxian area. It was found that these bandits had repeatedly committed robberies in Heyi Township, Fengxian Bridge, Lu Family , Buzheng Township, and Ouchi Tou in September and December of last year, and had injured the victims with knives, and had also committed kidnapping in Shuangshi Port in Dinghai County. They were successively arrested by the Ningbo Public Security Bureau, the Yinxian County Government, and the Fisheries Police Bureau, and were sent to the Security Command for interrogation. The confessions were confirmed to be true, and they were sentenced to death. The sentences were submitted to the higher authorities for approval. On that day, a team was dispatched to take the bandits from the detention center, verify their identities, and escort them to the execution ground to be executed by firing squad.

Female Performer Yao Shuijuan Assassinated 103

Female performer Yao Shuijuan, 22 years old, has performed in the Yinxian and Shaoxing areas, and enjoys great popularity. Recently, she went to Wenzhou, and fell in love with a local gentry, which caused jealousy, and she was attacked, dying on the spot. The identity of the murderer is being investigated by the local Public Security Bureau. Yao's artistic skills were excellent, and those who heard about it were saddened.

Huzhou: Shanlian Town Plundered by Bandits 104

At approximately 2 PM on the 6th, in Shanlian Town, the fourth district of Wuxing County, over seventy lake bandits from the Chaohu and Haizhou gangs suddenly arrived, divided among three Wushan boats, each carrying guns and weapons. They landed on the shore and first went to the town's security team, shooting down the door guards, and swarmed inside. All of the team's quick guns (18), wooden-cased guns (3), and pistols (1) were confiscated. The bandits then divided and plundered Taicheng Pawnshop, Yuantai Native Products Store, and various tobacco and paper shops, etc., looting over thirty establishments, with none spared. The total loss for the town is estimated at over 100,000 yuan. After the bandits looted, they fired their guns several times, lined up, got on their boats, and sailed out of the town's main harbor. A steamship from Pingwang to Xinshi happened to pass by and was seized by the bandits, who forced it to tow the three bandit boats towards Taihu Lake. Afterwards, the town's security team's chief reported the incident to the Wuzhen and Lian City military and police agencies by telephone. After receiving the report, the dispatched teams went to the scene, but there was no trace of the bandits. The Wuxing County Government, upon hearing the news, also ordered detective team members to go and investigate.

Shaoxing: Requesting Flexible Recompilation of Housing Tax 105

The Shaoxing County Government's recompilation of shop and residence tax has encountered many obstacles and difficulties. The people have repeatedly appealed. Yesterday, the County Chamber of Commerce, the Yue Society Lawyers Association, and other groups jointly submitted a report to the county, stating the local situation and requesting that the compilation and valuation be divided into two steps. First, focus on compiling omissions and concealed properties without setting high targets. After the people have recovered slightly, continue to discuss appropriate measures. County Magistrate He replied that the purpose of this compilation of shop and residence tax is to find out omissions and concealed properties, and to correct deviations, just as the public notice said, the tax amount compilation will be transferred according to the current situation, not to increase it as a fixed principle, and that in today's situation of people's poverty and commercial difficulty, we must urgently seek improvement. The estimated problem of how to weigh the times, once the matter is completed, will be to call together all the gentlemen and associations to the meeting to make a final decision.

Rural Life Miscellany 106

— Edited by Yu Qingtan

Rural Life in Jiujiang (Part 2) Jiang Aiqun

Farmers' Sideline Occupations

In terms of farmers' sideline occupations, women, besides a small number who work in places like the Jiuxing Yarn Factory and the Zhonghua Match Company in town, mostly stay at home, acting as virtuous wives and good mothers. Industrious and frugal farm families take pasting matchboxes as their only sideline occupation. For pasting 1,000 matchboxes, they only receive 400 cash. Often, the entire family, old and young, is kept busy, and they still have to pay for the labor of transporting the paste, twine, and delivering and picking up the matchboxes to earn anything. It seems like the match factory is too harsh. Actually, these local match factories are being encroached upon by the foreign match industry and are still struggling to survive in the face of adversity. So, it is probably more accurate to say that this is one piece of evidence of the deep penetration of imperialist forces into the countryside. Men cannot rely solely on farmland. As we saw in the previous section about the poverty of farmers cultivating farmland, we can imagine that their major income comes from carrying loads and carrying sedan chairs in Lushan. If we say that carrying loads and carrying sedan chairs is their main occupation, there is some justification for that. The price for carrying loads (from Jiujiang to Guling is 43 li) is 3 strings of cash per 100 jin. Valuable items that need to be carefully protected can be increased to 1 or 2 strings of cash. Farmers who carry sedan chairs are half from Jiujiang and half from Huangmei. The price for carrying sedan chairs (from Lianhua Cave at the foot of Lushan to Guling, a mountain road of 18 li) is 4 yuan in legal tender per sedan chair, with each of the four carriers getting one yuan. Because the sedan chairs belong to the China Travel Service, each person has to pay a rent of 2 jiao. They often carry foreigners, so they can say a few English words, such as "dollars", "yes", and "number one," etc. A few years ago, there were 4,000 to 5,000 people engaged in these two sideline occupations. In recent years, there are only 2,000 to 3,000. Business is busiest from May to September each year. If business is good, each person can earn a net profit of 100 yuan per year. If business is not good, they can still earn a net profit of 50 to 60 yuan, which is also a considerable help to their household expenses. However, when they are working, under the scorching sun, going up and down the mountain, those who take summer vacation in Lushan should imagine how much hardship and danger there is! Midway up the mountain, there is a place called "Hero's Slope". The mountain is steep and difficult to climb. It is said that one who passes this slope is a hero. If we give this beautiful name to these farmers, they truly deserve it without shame! In addition, selling firewood is also an important sideline occupation, but because of the limited space, I will not say more about it.

Farmers' Conscription and Corvee Labor

In recent years, in addition to the serious losses caused by severe floods and droughts, the most painful thing for farmers is the government's conscription and corvee labor. The situation of the people's corvee labor in each bao in the past three years is as follows: In January of the 23rd year, to build the Jiuxing Road (Jiujiang to Xingzi), over 100 laborers were conscripted. In June of the 24th year, over 30 laborers were additionally conscripted. In March of the 23rd year, to build the airport, over 300 laborers were conscripted. In October of the same year, to build the Jiurui Road (Jiujiang to Ruichang), over 400 laborers were conscripted. In March of the 24th year, over 100 laborers were again conscripted for repairs. In October of the 24th year, to build the Lianxi Road, over 200 laborers were conscripted (some added to the river dredging and river filling project to make over 1,000 laborers). In January of the 25th year, to build the Jiuhu Road (Jiujiang to Hukou), over 600 laborers were conscripted, as well as over 100 laborers conscripted for other repairs of bridges and transportation of timber miscellaneous work. In total, there are no less than 2,000 laborers conscripted (an average of 20 laborers per household). Some farm families hire people to be conscripted in their place, which must bear a very heavy labor wages. Those who cannot afford to hire people to be conscripted have to go into service themselves. Often, the whole family, old and young, rely on him to carry burdens to maintain their livelihoods. At this time, they have to put aside their own family's food and clothing problems and go to serve. Moreover, because the conscription site is far away, it usually takes 10 days or 8 days to return. Then, not only can they not earn money to maintain the family's livelihood, but they have to beg and plead with high-interest lenders to borrow some money to buy rice and salt and bring it to the conscription site for use through the door of heavy interest exploitation. Recently, it has been rumored that the province is subsidizing 100,000 yuan in labor costs for the construction of the Jiuxing, Jiuhu, and Jiurui roads, but after it arrives at the local government, they say that it is used for surveying and office work, or that it is reserved for bridge and water pipe needs, with various excuses to prevaricate the farmers. The farmers sacrificed their own work and paid for firewood and rice to be conscripted, which has already caused great losses. Should the surveying fees and bridge and water pipe fees also be borne by the farmers? In short, the people of Jiangxi have suffered years of devastation by the communists. As in the great drought years ago, the crops were almost completely barren, and the people have been emptied out. They urgently need to recuperate. The government must pay special attention to this. (End)

Local News

Official and Merchant Handling of Smuggling 107

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs replied to the Chamber of Commerce. The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce received a reply telegram from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Ya-zi No. 5368, yesterday, which said: "To the Shanghai National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, your telegram has been noted. Regarding the increase of Japanese troops in North China and the smuggling by Japanese and Korean ruffians, this Ministry has repeatedly lodged protests with the Japanese side, demanding that they stop increasing troops in China and strictly crack down on Japanese and Korean smuggling criminals. The central government has now established strict investigation and suppression measures for smuggling and has instructed the competent authorities to rigorously implement them. This is a special reply. [Signed] Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Qi."

The Customs Bureau Auctions a Large Quantity of Smuggled Sugar. The Jianghai Customs Bureau issued a notice the day before yesterday, stating: "This Customs Bureau currently has 467 bags of fine white sugar, weighing 37.145 kilograms; another 2,517 bags, weighing 206.394 kilograms; 600 bags of white sugar, weighing 59.400 kilograms; 300 bags of brown sugar, weighing 21.700 kilograms; and 832 boxes of rock sugar, weighing 23.870 kilograms, for which bids are invited. Bids for the entire quantity or only a portion are acceptable. The weights listed above are approximate; accurate weights can be determined by re-weighing upon collection. During the bidding period, from 9:00 a.m. to 4:30 p.m. daily, bidders may personally apply to the Transportation Department of this Customs Bureau to inspect the goods and obtain samples. Bids must be submitted to the Taxation Department of the General Affairs Section of this Customs Bureau before 10:00 a.m. on the 18th of this month (Thursday). This Customs Bureau reserves the right not to accept the highest bid or any bid. The successful bidder shall submit 25% of the bid price to the Customs Bureau on the same day and pay the remaining balance within two weeks to collect the goods from the Customs Bureau's Pudong Warehouse. This notice is hereby given. June 8, 25th year of the Republic of China. [Signed] Tax Commissioner, P. Bairnson."

Fish Industry Group's Secret Inspection

The Fish Industry Anti-Smuggling Inspection Committee, after announcing its establishment previously, dispatched personnel to various districts yesterday for secret inspections to determine whether fish merchants were smuggling goods. The organizational regulations of the Inspection Committee are as follows: 1. This committee is organized by all members of the marine fish industry and is named the Shanghai Fish Industry Anti-Smuggling Inspection Committee. 2. The purpose of this committee is to assist the government in strictly organizing the fish industry, strengthening anti-smuggling efforts, and respecting national sovereignty. 3. All fishermen, fish merchants, aquaculture, refrigeration, customs declaration, transportation, and other related patriotic comrades may join this committee as members. 4. The committee shall have fifteen members, five standing members, one chairman, one secretary, and a number of staff members dedicated to anti-smuggling inspection work. 5. The expenses of this committee shall be borne by the members themselves. 6. Upon discovery of smuggling, this committee shall immediately report it to the Customs Bureau for disposal. 7. After verification of the reported smuggled goods, in addition to requesting rewards from the Customs Bureau, this committee shall also provide honorary rewards. 8. Reporters, whether from the fish industry or outside, shall not fabricate facts based on personal grudges to harm others. 9. If staff members are found to be colluding, concealing, accepting bribes, or releasing goods, they shall be reported to the relevant authorities and punished as principal offenders and accomplices. 10. For the convenience of inspection, this committee may establish branch offices, and the directors of the offices shall be elected separately. 11. These regulations shall be implemented upon approval by the committee and may be amended at any time if there are any imperfections. The committee also sent a telegram to the national fish industry, stating: "Since Japanese ruffians have taken advantage of the special forces in North China to engage in organized smuggling, it has become like a rushing river, flooding the entire country. Its harm not only causes a large loss of tax revenue for our Customs Bureau but also rapidly destroys our economic structure, which is a million times more serious than military aggression. Although the government has now strictly established anti-smuggling measures to curb this in the future, some unscrupulous people still do not hesitate to act as accomplices, exhausting their ability to exploit loopholes and find outlets for smuggled goods everywhere. Thinking of this, how can we not be filled with fear? As far as our fish industry is concerned, the fishery products of seven provinces are being arbitrarily invaded by them. Even the obtained fishery products are disguised as domestic products and sold in large quantities, depriving our fishermen of their livelihoods. This has been happening not just for a day or two, and in the future, it will inevitably become more and more serious, and they will also smuggle their own imported goods on a large scale. Our colleagues, aware of this, have united with the backbone members of the industry to establish the Shanghai Fish Industry Anti-Smuggling Inspection Committee and have issued a declaration to begin inspection work. We hope that the people of the whole country and all industry groups, mindful of the current crisis, will stand on the same front, assist the government, eliminate traitors, and act quickly to save ourselves, which is the task of the nation and the first sign of unity. We respectfully offer our humble sincerity and hope for your public consideration. (Dagong News Agency)"

Electrical Appliance Industry Petitions the Ministry of Finance

The Shanghai Electrical Appliance Manufacturing Industry Association submitted a document to the Ministry of Finance, stating: "Regarding the petition to amend the regulations on punishing smuggling, in addition to punishing the principal offenders, also punish important related persons, and respectfully request your approval. Since the issue of smuggling arose, tax revenue has been lost, and all industries are in panic, affecting the national economy and people's livelihoods in a very serious way. Your Ministry is well aware of the seriousness of the situation, and that rigorous suppression is necessary to turn the tide. Therefore, you issued clear orders and established regulations to punish smuggling, and various industry associations have also gathered to discuss and automatically report smuggling, so the trend of smuggling has been slightly curbed. However, given our country's environment, there are still those who invoke special forces to continue smuggling. Therefore, fundamental prevention is still difficult to fully realize. It is suggested that the punishment regulations be supplemented, and in addition to punishing the principal offenders according to the law, other important related persons should also be punished according to the severity of their responsibility, so that the sale and purchase of smuggled goods is not easy to operate, and although the smugglers are unscrupulous, the connection relationships can create direct resistance, and since the related persons must bear the punishment, the smugglers have to share their profits to silence them, so indirectly the smugglers' profits can be reduced, and they will not be willing to do this illegal thing. If this can be done, the power to prevent smuggling can be increased invisibly, and the purpose of fundamentally clearing up the problem can be achieved sooner. This is what the members of this association hope for. We respectfully submit our shallow views to your Ministry for inspection and hope for your approval, and we await your orders with utmost anxiety. Respectfully presented to Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance."

The Ministry of Railways has completed the entire Jiangnan Railway line, and the section from Sunjiabu to Quzhou will be built first to connect with the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway. 110

The Jiangnan Railway Company, founded by Zhang Jingjiang and others, is the pioneer of private railway enterprises in China. The first plan was to build the Wuhu-Zhapu Railway from Wuhu, Anhui to Zhapu, Zhejiang. The section from Wuhu to Sunjiabu in Xuancheng was started first and was opened to traffic in the 23rd year. In the 24th year, the shareholders' meeting decided to change the construction plan from Nanjing, through Wuhu, Xuancheng, Huizhou, Quzhou, to Anhui, Zhejiang, and Fujian provinces, and to Zhao'an on the Guangdong border, and was renamed the Jingzhao Railway. It was submitted to the Ministry of Railways for approval, with 30 years of operating rights. The first section to be built was a public network from Nanjing to Wuhu, which was opened to traffic last year and connected to the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway this spring. Passenger and freight transportation is busy, making it a major trunk line of the Jiangnan Railway network. The company is currently planning to extend the line from Sunjiabu to Huizhou, but it must submit a proposal to the shareholders' meeting to raise additional funds before it can proceed. According to the person in charge of the company, the Ministry of Railways now considers the road to be important and urgently needs to complete the entire line. Therefore, it decided to recover it for state operation and build the section from Sunjiabu to Quzhou first to connect with the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway. The company has received an order from the Ministry and immediately sent it to General Manager Zhang Jingjiang for review and submission to the shareholders' meeting for a decision. Zhang originally proposed that the road be privately operated, mainly to assist the government's construction with the people's resources. Now that the government intends to take it over for state operation, it will comply with the order and cede it. However, the Jing-Wu section that has already been opened to traffic was originally invested by the company and has achieved good results, so it will still be privately operated. In the future, after the completion and opening of the Chu-Qu section, joint transportation will be carried out with the Ministry of Railways. Jingdian said that the road will be purchased by the Ministry and that all conditions have been largely agreed upon. The company denied this.

China Aviation's Shanghai-Pingjin Line Aircraft Fly Round Trip on the Same Day, Leaving Shanghai at 6:00 a.m. and Returning to Shanghai at 7:00 p.m. 111

China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Pingjin route will, from yesterday, be changed to round-trip flights on the same day to facilitate passengers. China Flying Club Training Class Holds Opening Ceremony on Schedule, and a Tea Party was Held Last Night. 112

After the announcement of the enrollment of students in the first flying training class of the China Flying Club, preparations for the opening of the class are being actively carried out. The club held a tea party at the YMCA in the Banzian Bridge at 5:00 p.m. to connect the feelings of the students and discuss the progress. All members and the club's Secretary-General Yao Xijiu, Aircraft and Navigation Group Director Chen Buzhou, etc. attended. Yao introduced each student and then reported on the purpose and process of establishing the flying class, saying that the opening of the flying training class is to promote civil aviation, so that people have a considerable understanding, as the initial step in the development of civil aviation, and to reserve talents for the government. The course is roughly the same as the primary flying class of the aviation school. As for the process of establishment, after the government approved the articles of association in mid-August last year, it formulated the course, etc., and announced its establishment in October, and ordered aircraft, and at the same time carried out publicity in writing. The aircraft will be delivered this spring, and the class can be opened. As for the tuition fee of 600 yuan, it is based on the estimated fuel costs, instructor salaries, and miscellaneous expenses incurred by the students. Because the club has no subsidies from the government, it is entirely borne by the students. In the future, if there are achievements and the government has subsidies, the burden on the students can be reduced. Regarding the students' future, according to government orders, the examination in the future must be handled in accordance with the Flying Personnel Examination Regulations, and personnel will be sent to supervise the examination. The regulations are strict, but the qualifications can be in line with primary pilots. Please provide proof, or send them to aviation schools to continue their studies, or introduce them to work in civil aviation companies. Then, it was agreed that half of the tuition fee should be paid within this week, and the rest should be paid in installments, but a guarantor is required, and it must be paid off within three months after the start of school. The opening ceremony will be held at the Longhua Flying Port on the morning of the 18th. At that time, Aviation Association Director Wu, the mayor, etc. will be invited to attend and give instructions. The opening of flight training is scheduled for the 22nd.

More than 30 Trade Associations Petition the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to Postpone the Payment of Overdue Fees 113

More than 30 trade associations in this city, including the Qing Oil and Flower Cake Industry, Bamboo Industry, Sand and Gravel Industry, Fenjiu Industry, Kitchenware Industry, Flower and Tree Industry, Sesame Oil Industry, Machine-Made Noodles Industry, Fishing Boat Sand Transportation Industry, Parasol Industry, Garment Industry, Printing and Dyeing Industry, Flour Industry, Cotton Ginning Industry, Hot Water Bottle Manufacturing Industry, Fresh Medicine Industry, Pollen Industry, Tin Printing and Can Manufacturing Industry, Silk and Satin Printing Industry, Canned Candy, Biscuit, and Bread Industry, Vegetables, Paint and Woodware Industry, etc., jointly petitioned the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, requesting to change the articles of association, postpone the payment of overdue membership fees, and allow the election of representatives to attend the general meeting to facilitate commercial operations. The document states: "Regarding the request to remedy the rights of members, change the procedures of the articles of association, postpone the payment of overdue membership fees, and allow the election of representatives to attend the meeting, there are four reasons why the affiliated associations have overdue membership fees. 1. The source of income for the affiliated associations depends entirely on the membership fees received from each member. However, the method of requiring compulsory membership cannot be implemented, so the associations cannot control the members of the same industry, and the members who have joined use this as an excuse and are unwilling to pay membership fees. This is one of the reasons why the affiliated associations have overdue fees. 2. The industry regulations of each industry association are drafted with reference to the interests of each industry. Every time they are submitted for record, the important clauses are deleted by the superior, resulting in mediocre industry regulations. The members are unwilling to pay membership fees because they see that the industry regulations are equivalent to a mere formality. This is the second reason why the affiliated associations have overdue fees. 3. The members of each association are unable to approve the industry regulations that are being submitted, and those that have been approved cannot be implemented. It is especially difficult in the concession areas, resulting in the industry regulations not taking effect, and the members' business operations are not guaranteed, so they are unwilling to pay fees. This is the third reason why the affiliated associations have overdue fees. 4. Each industry is affected by the whirlpool of the sluggish market, and business is in a slump. For price reductions, dumping, etc., each association is unable to rectify them because of the non-membership relationship, resulting in the members who have joined using the excuse that non-members cannot be controlled and business operations cannot be guaranteed, so they are unwilling to pay fees. This is the fourth reason why the affiliated associations have overdue fees. In summary, the above four reasons have put the affiliated associations in a helpless financial situation. Therefore, we specially jointly petition for a change of procedures, request a postponement of fee payments, and allow the election of representatives, so that the above reasons can be submitted to the general meeting for discussion of effective measures, so that the public associations that are struggling to survive can reach a state of completion and avoid the concerns of being strong on the outside but weak on the inside. This is really for the public convenience. Respectfully presented to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce."

Shanghai Syndicate Handles Anhui Province Agricultural Warehouse Loan, Contract for a Total of 4.4 Million to be Signed, 100 Warehouses to be Completed Before the Autumn Harvest 116

In order to regulate the rural economy of Anhui Province and develop agricultural production, the Anhui Provincial Government, after establishing the Agricultural Warehouse Management Office, has negotiated with the Bank of China, the China Farmers Bank, and the China Agricultural Loan Syndicate, and has reached an agreement to jointly invest 4.4 million yuan to handle storage and mortgage loans. The contract will be signed soon. The details are as follows:

Handling Storage and Mortgage Loans. After the Anhui Provincial Government established the Agricultural Warehouse Management Office based on the resolutions of the Rural Economic Research Conference, it dispatched Secretary Hu Shiqi to Shanghai several times to contact the banking community in the city for storage and mortgage loans in order to realize the plan to revive the rural economy of Anhui Province. After many rounds of consultations, a basic decision has been made that the Bank of China, the China Farmers Bank, and the China Agricultural Cooperative Loan Syndicate will jointly handle storage and mortgage loans, with a total amount of 4.4 million yuan. The Bank of China and the China Farmers Bank will each recognize 1.7 million yuan, and the China Agricultural Cooperative Loan Syndicate will recognize 1 million yuan, totaling 4.4 million yuan. The interest rate is 8% per month. The Agricultural Warehouse Management Office of the Anhui Provincial Government will build agricultural warehouses. The contracts have been negotiated and will be formally signed soon.

Regional Divisions Specified. Warehouse construction is divided into two types: provincial warehouses and county warehouses. It is planned to build a total of 100 warehouses. In addition to renovating existing warehouses, the remaining locations have been surveyed and construction has begun. All are limited to completion before this year's autumn harvest. The storage and mortgage loan areas have also been specified. 1. The China Agricultural Loan Syndicate is responsible for 23 counties, including Qimen, Fengyang, Nanling, Chaoxian, Wuwei, Wuhe, Lingbi, Shitai, Jingde, Jixi, Yixian, Langxi, Guangde, Ningguo, Jingxian, Taiping, Qingyang, Guichi, Tianchang, Quanjiao, Boxian, Fuyang, and Yingshang. 2. The Bank of China is responsible for 12 counties, including Xuancheng, Dangtu, Hexian, Fanchang, Jinshan, Suxian, Chuxian, Dingyuan, Woyang, Mengcheng, Laian, and Jiashan. 3. The China Farmers Bank is responsible for 12 counties, including Wuhu, Huaining, Tongcheng, Tongling, Lujiang, Hefei, Shucheng, Shou County, Huaiyuan, Fengtai, Huoqiu, and Xiuning. It was decided to divide the work and cooperate to jointly handle the matter.

Page 11

Zeng Yangfu Inspects Zhejiang Cocoon Area, Spring Cocoon Harvest is Abundant, Cocoon Quality is Good, Unified Committee Collects Cocoons, Reels Them, and then Promotes Them Overseas, From Next Year Onward, Our Country Can Be Self-Sufficient in Silkworm Eggs, Detention of Spring Cocoons for Shipment Has Been Released 118

Zeng Yiafu, Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Sericulture Control Committee, has completed his inspection of the cocoon-producing areas in Zhejiang. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency specially visited Zeng yesterday and was informed of the details of this year's cocoon production in Zhejiang. The details are as follows:

Abundant Spring Cocoon Harvest

After the new cocoons entered the market this year, Zeng went to inspect the cocoon-producing areas in Zhejiang, and the development of improved breeds and the quantity of cocoons produced in various places were very good. The improved seeds issued in Zhejiang Province amounted to about 1.2 million sheets, with an average cocoon yield of more than 30 catties. Therefore, the total output of spring cocoons in Zhejiang Province this year was about 360,000 dan of fresh cocoons for improved breeds and about 180,000 dan of fresh cocoons for native breeds. As for the quality of improved cocoons in Jiaxing, Wuxing, Yuji, Lin'an and other places, most of them are very good, with a reeling waste of less than 400 catties. The cocoon quality in Wukang, Chongde and other places is relatively poor, because they are relatively close to the native seed production area in Yuyao. The reeling waste is about 450 catties.

Unified Committee Collects Cocoons

In order to help farmers, the Sericulture Control Committee borrowed 5 million yuan from the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications to purchase the remaining cocoons in Zhejiang Province this spring. The collection of cocoons is handled by the Spring Cocoon Collection Committee in the 25th year. As expected, the spring cocoon harvest this year was abundant. Although silk merchants and remaining cocoon merchants absorbed as much as possible, there was still a surplus of about 100,000 dan of fresh cocoons, which were all purchased by the Unified Committee. The collected cocoons are issued to the silk reeling committee, and the 3,000 new-style silk reeling machines of the Zhejiang Silk Factory, which are guided by the Unified Committee, are used to reel silk. The reeled silk is sold by the raw silk promotion office. Most of it is still sold through Shanghai exporters as in the previous year, and a part is sold directly to foreign markets by the promotion office.

Balancing Cocoon Prices

The Cocoon Control Committee stipulated the central cocoon price for silk merchants and remaining cocoon merchants to purchase spring cocoons this year. The negotiated price for improved breeds was 30 yuan, and the negotiated price for native breeds was 21 yuan. At the same time, it strictly prohibited raising or suppressing prices. Later, it was reported that most of the cocoon merchants purchased cocoons in accordance with this central cocoon price, but some of the negotiated prices were slightly lower. The provincial government paid great attention to protecting farmers. For the cocoons that had been collected, those with a negotiated price below the central cocoon price were withheld by 40% and samples were taken for testing. If the reeling waste is large and the purchase price is low, and the proportion is calculated to be consistent with the 550 catties of the stipulated central cocoon price, there is no problem because it is the same as the principles reviewed by the Unified Committee.

Self-Sufficiency in Seed Production

This year, the improved spring cocoon seeds in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces issued about 400,000 sheets, which were ordered from abroad. The cocoons produced by these seeds are of very good quality. The Jiaxing branch seed production farm, which was established by the Zhejiang Unified Committee, is actively proceeding. It is expected that from next year onwards, our country can be self-sufficient in silkworm eggs and will not have to purchase them from abroad. It is expected that next year's spring seeds will produce 3.5 million sheets in our country. If each sheet produces 30 catties of cocoons, the two provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang can produce more than 1 million dan of cocoons, not to mention the native breeds. Now farmers have great faith in improved breeds, so it is expected that native breeds will gradually decrease from next year onwards.

Release of Detained Cocoons

The Zhejiang Provincial Sericulture Control Committee, under the order of the provincial government, detained the silk merchants and remaining cocoon merchants who purchased spring cocoons in Zhejiang Province if their negotiated prices were below the standard number (21 yuan for native breeds and 30 yuan for improved breeds). The Shanghai Silk Factory Abandonment Association telegraphed to request the release. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency learned from Shanghai silk merchants yesterday that the cocoons that had been detained by the Zhejiang Sericulture Control Committee have been released as counted, and samples have been taken for testing the reeling waste to determine the method of disposal and urging. In the future, the fines will be deducted from the guarantee deposits of the cocoon merchants.

Lawyers' Association Exposes Negligence of Supervision by Banks and Native Banks, Offering No Practical Benefit to Creditors, Should be Reprimanded, and Husband and Horse Expenses Recovered 123

The Shanghai Lawyers' Association submitted a document to the Executive Yuan's Ministry of Finance, stating that, according to a proposal by member Xu Zuoliang and others, since the government promulgated the "Supervision and Liquidation Measures for Banks and Native Banks," it has appointed one supervisor for each of the Shanghai banks and native banks that have ceased operations, with the banks or native banks giving them preferential monthly husband and horse expenses of 200 or 300 yuan. This money is for the repayment of debts, but giving it preferentially to the supervisor has actually caused losses to the creditors. If the supervisors could truly break through sentiments and fulfill their responsibilities in accordance with the provisions of the measures, the creditors would be willing to endure it for the sake of jointly protecting their interests. However, in reality, it is the opposite. Specifically: According to the second clause of the measures, the liquidation is limited to three months from the date of suspension of operations. However, each of the liquidators has been in office for more than a year in most cases, and at least six months in a few, without ever convening a creditors' meeting or reporting in detail the property inventory and loan comparison table of the bank or native bank. They are simply holding their positions without doing anything, which is a dereliction of duty. According to the third clause of the measures, if any managers or directors are found to have engaged in illegal or fraudulent activities during the liquidation period, they should be placed under custody and dealt with according to law. However, all of the closed banks and native banks in Shanghai were caused by illegal or fraudulent activities by managers and directors, and some victims have even filed lawsuits and been sentenced by the court. However, no supervisor has been heard to have reported or placed the managers or directors under custody and punished them according to law. Recently, it was reported that after the collapse of Meifeng Bank, the liquidator reported that the manager Lei Wen was sentenced to imprisonment. However, the directors and supervisors of all the Chinese banks and native banks that have ceased operations are still at large. Some say that the protection of creditors by Chinese people is not as thorough as that by Westerners, which is not without reason. According to the fourth clause of the measures, after the assets are discounted, if they are not sufficient to offset the liabilities, in addition to limited liability companies that should be declared bankrupt, the shareholders and managers of other banks and native banks should bear joint liability. According to the fifth clause, if there is any intention to escape or conceal or reduce property, they may be placed under custody or wanted. However, after the suspension of operations of the various banks and native banks in Shanghai, many assets have been evaded or destroyed, and the liquidators have not taken preventive measures beforehand, nor have they heard of any punishment afterwards, which is of no practical benefit to creditors. Based on the members' limited views, it is believed that the position of liquidator is stipulated by the liquidation measures and cannot be compared with ordinary concurrent positions that only receive dry salaries without doing anything. It is appropriate to request correction and immediately reprimand the negligent liquidators and supervisors, and recover the husband and horse expenses as a warning. Therefore, this request is submitted for your examination and approval so that you may correct the situation to relieve the business distress and maintain creditors’ rights in a fair manner. Respectfully submitted to Director Jiang of the Executive Yuan. Respectfully submitted by the Standing Committee of the Shanghai Lawyers' Association. It is heard that the Secretariat of the Executive Yuan has replied to the Association yesterday, briefly stating that it has been sent to the Ministry of Finance for investigation. Please be informed.

Resolution of the Far East Factory Strike - Workers Remaining at the Factory Resumed Work Yesterday - 110 Workers Approved for Dismissal - Dismissal Pay to be Issued by the Labor and Capital Sides on the Basis of Name 124

The British-owned Belle Company (i.e., Far East Sawmill) experienced a strike dispute due to sluggish business and the dismissal of Chinese workers, which has lasted for two months. The dispute has been resolved after mediation by the Social and Public Security Bureaus, with a settlement record signed. Workers resumed work yesterday. The settlement methods are recorded as follows: Due to the sluggish business of the factory, 110 workers including Yin Xiuhuai, etc., are approved for dismissal; Long-term workers will be given one month's wages as dismissal pay, plus half a month's travel expenses; Temporary workers will be given one month's wages as dismissal pay; The factory will be responsible for ensuring that workers remaining at the factory work at least 18 days per month; Workers remaining at the factory will resume work immediately after the dismissal.

Chinese and Foreign Relief Federation - Completion of Road Construction by Xuzhou Work Relief 126

The China Chinese and Foreign Relief and Disaster Relief Federation at No. 505 Henan Road, in order to relieve the disaster victims in northern Jiangsu, specially allocated funds to carry out work relief and established the Northern Jiangsu Yellow Disaster Work Relief Office to supervise it. It was originally planned to repair the Weishan Lake embankment and the Xuzhou-Haizhou highway, but due to the vast yellow water in the Weihu area, construction could not be carried out. Therefore, the original plan was changed to only repair the Xuhai highways in Xuzhou and Haizhou, and the route was extended. The Xuzhou side was presided over by Pastor Peng Yong'en in the local area, and the Haizhou side was requested to be organized by Pastor Hu Lelin. Engineer Zhang Jichun was also sent to plan and supervise the projects in both places. Since construction began simultaneously in February of this year, the roads built in Xuzhou, in addition to the ten-li around-the-city road, also included five highways, namely: Tongpei Road, from Beimen Bridge to Zhengji, is fifty li long and is an important transportation route from Xuzhou to Tongpei Feng. Passing through Ping Shankou, the road surface is very high, and it is very difficult for trains to go up and down, and they often overturn and injure people. The Yamaguchi was blown down by two zhang with dynamite, widened by one zhang, and opened into a wide road to facilitate travel. The road is paved with crushed stones, and three stone bridges are built, which is the most expensive of the roads built. Tong Sui Road, from Chengnan to Liangshankou, is thirty li long. The road is located in the old course of the Yellow River and is purely loose and less soil-like, which is inconvenient for vehicles to pass. Now, red clay from Yunlong Mountain is used, mixed with one-third of sandy soil, to build the road surface, and the motor vehicle and ox cart lanes are paved separately. Because the clay is taken from other places, mining and transportation are very troublesome. Tong Dang Road, from Chengxi to Hao'an, is thirty li long; Tong Su Road, from Chengnan to Sanguan Temple, is ten li long; Tong Xiao Road, from Chengbei to Yaolou, is thirty li long. The width of each road is 12 meters as stipulated by the Provincial Construction Department, which can accommodate motor vehicles and ox carts, and the upper and lower lanes are driven separately, with drainage ditches on both sides to facilitate drainage. The encircling road has been badly damaged, and it has now been renovated. The road construction in Haizhou is from Xiangshuikou to Banpu, passing through Tongxingji Yangjiaji, with a total of three sections, and then northwest from Banpu to Xinpu, a total of one hundred and twenty li long. Half of the old roads are repaired and half are newly built. Between Banpu and Xinpu, the embankment is repaired and reinforced along the river. The width of this road is the same as that built in Xuzhou, which is very important to the traffic in northern Jiangsu. Because Xiangshuikou is located at the mouth of the Dachao River, land and sea transportation can be connected after it is built, and it can be connected to the highway passing through Dongkan Funing and arriving at Jiancheng. In Xinpu, it can also be connected to the highway passing through Haizhou Shuyang to Qingjiangpu. The work relief this time requires approximately 45,000 yuan in Xuzhou and approximately 27,000 yuan in Haizhou. The purpose is to relieve the disaster, and construction is the price. Therefore, more than 2,500 disaster workers are employed, regardless of their strength or weakness. Strong men are ordered to be responsible for the arduous tasks of opening roads in the mountains, while the old and weak only sit and hit gravel, which is easy and convenient. The average wage per person is 25 cents a day, so as to provide a simple life for individuals and families. It is reported that the Haizhou road project is progressing slowly due to the continuous spring rain and the construction of river dikes, and the completion date is still uncertain. However, Xuzhou has been completed last week, and the completion ceremony is scheduled to be held on the 12th of this month. Local officials and representatives from all walks of life will be invited to participate, and the test drive will be carried out together, and then the opening will be accepted by the Jiangsu Provincial Government and the Tong District Commissioner.

Zhaoshangju requests in the Li Guojie case: Investigate Guarantor Assets in Detail; If the Guarantor Fails to Provide Sufficient Assets, Request the Case to be Summoned and Arrested to Pursue the Defendant's Debt 133

The case of the state-owned Zhaoshangju being embezzled of public funds of 700,000 taels by Li Guojie has been concluded by the final trial of the High Court. The judgment was final, ordering Li Guojie to compensate the full amount, including interest, totaling more than 1 million yuan. The Bureau entrusted lawyer Jiang Hechun to appear in court as an agent for the execution of the case transmitted on the 6th of this month, requesting that the defendant Li Guojie continue to be detained and execute the compensation payment. The court ruled that He De and Li Sihao acted as guarantors for Li Guojie's release and were required to ensure that he was available whenever summoned. If he failed to appear when summoned, the guarantors would be responsible for all debts. Now, the Zhaoshangju believes that the national currency is no small matter, in order to clarify the responsibilities of the guarantors and request the defendant to quickly list his assets and submit them to the case for payment, it has again sent a letter to the court. The original text is excerpted above. To the Jiangsu Shanghai Local Court: In the state-owned Zhaoshangju's lawsuit against Li Guojie for embezzlement of public funds, the attached civil suit for compensation for losses has been finalized by the final trial, ordering Li Guojie to compensate the Zhaoshangju with 700,000 Shanghai taels, plus interest, etc. On the 6th of this month, the execution of the case transmitted was received, and lawyer Jiang Hechun was entrusted as an agent to appear in court, requesting that the defendant Li Guojie continue to be detained and execute the compensation payment, and the authorized agent lawyer solemnly declared repeatedly in court that the matter belonged to public funds, the case was of great importance, and it should be submitted to the Ministry of Communications for instructions. Your court ruled that Li Guojie was allowed to be released on bail by He De (i.e., Qiaqing) and Li Sihao (Zanhou), and the guarantors were to bear full responsibility for the case if Li Guojie failed to appear in the future, and it was also recorded in court that the guarantors signed and acknowledged it. The decision to detain or release the defendant on bail is the jurisdiction of the court, and our bureau should respect it. However, the circumstances of this case are serious, the amount of debt is huge, and it is related to national property. It is, of course, no small matter, and the attention of China and foreign countries is extensive. The guarantors, in their personal capacity, bear the heavy responsibility of guaranteeing such a huge amount of debt. Whether their financial resources are sufficient to bear this responsibility is a matter that our bureau cannot but solemnly declare and should request the court to carefully investigate and review, ordering the guarantors to provide sufficient proof to emphasize the responsibility of the guarantee. If the guarantors fail to provide sufficient assets to guarantee the amount owed by the defendant, we still request your court to summon and arrest the defendant to pursue the debt and emphasize the importance of public funds. As for the defendant's willingness to be released on bail and to investigate and provide all his assets for execution, it cannot be indefinite and beyond the law. Your court should order him to do so within one month to facilitate the execution, so that the facts can be dealt with and the public funds will not be without a source. It was stated to the agent in court yesterday, for fear that the record might not be fully restored, so as to facilitate the application for continued execution. If the approved period expires and the defendant still fails to declare his assets, your court should summon him to be detained according to law to emphasize public funds and extend legal rights. This is addressed to the Jiangsu Shanghai Local Court.

Song Xihou, a native of Yuyao who resided at No. , Sida Village, Lane 142, Rémusat Road, French Concession, and was the compradore of the Shanghai office of the British Hezhilin Cotton Yarn Company, was suddenly visited by two men in suits at noon the day before yesterday who brought a letter and asked to see him. Rickshaw Industry Association Opposes Modification of Wheels, Yesterday Sent a Letter to the Municipal Council Stating Various Reasons, Requesting a Halt to Implementation Based on Members' Opinions 136

The Shanghai Rickshaw Industry Mutual Aid Association, in order to oppose the modification of wheels, yesterday sent a letter to Zhong Si, the Director-General of the Public Concession Municipal Council, which stated, "Dear Sir, Regarding the matter of modifying the wheels of rickshaws, since your Bureau announced that it would be implemented on July 1 of this year, our members have felt significant obstacles in terms of business use and economy, and are deeply disturbed. They have requested that your Bureau be asked to stop the implementation. The reasons why the members find it impossible to accept are summarized as follows: The old-fashioned wheels of rickshaws are lightweight and suitable, and there has never been any problem with them. If the width is increased and the three-and-a-half-angle iron wheels are modified, they will inevitably be bulky and difficult to operate. If rubber tires are installed, the hardness will be uneven with the road surface, which will not only be inconvenient to use, but also the value of each set of rubber tires will be at least 16 yuan in national currency, and they can only be used for one year, while the old-fashioned wheels are only worth 3 yuan in national currency per set and can be guaranteed for more than ten years. The price is several times higher than the old-fashioned wheels. Even in terms of the cost of each rickshaw, it does not exceed 20 yuan. Now the value of one wheel is so high. In the current situation of a sluggish market and a declining business, how can people who earn a living with their blood and sweat bear this kind of burden suddenly? Therefore, in fact, it is impossible to accept either the modification of iron wheels or rubber tires. As for the issue of rickshaw load, because the restrictions are too strict, violations occur at every turn, and the suffering suffered in business is difficult to express. It should be requested that the load limit for single-person vehicles be 700 pounds, and the load limit for double-person vehicles be 1,000 pounds. Regarding the issue of modifying wheels, our association submitted a letter to your Bureau on December 5, 1935, to contribute opinions, and a reply was approved. Now the date for the regulation on modifying wheels is approaching, and the members are finding it difficult to maintain their livelihoods due to the sluggish business, and it is impossible to increase the unexpected burden again. Since we have been requested to come forward, we have prepared another letter to reach you. We urge your Bureau to consider the hardships of the workers, stop the implementation, and also handle the issue of load with flexibility. We hope you will investigate and reply to this letter. Sincerely, Zhong Si, Director-General of the Municipal Council."
