Enmity over Three Yuan, Thugs Kill Each Other, Jiang Xingsheng Stabbed to Death 140

Jiang Xingsheng, a native of Changzhou, 26 years old, who lived at No. 284, Fulili Road, French Concession, used to work at the Qiming Yarn Factory on Xietu Road, Dapu Bridge. He stopped working and idled, living a vagrant life with other hooligans and loafers nearby. Recently, a new store opened on Fulili Road, and Jiang went to negotiate a protection fee of three yuan. He did not receive it at the time. The next day, Jiang ordered a fellow hooligan named A Xiang to collect the money, but A Xiang kept it for himself, which led to a feud between the two. The day before yesterday (8th), at 9:00 a.m., A Xiang went to Jiang's house to ask Jiang for a loan, but failed. At 7:00 p.m., A Xiang went to Jiang's house again and lured Jiang out. In a secluded place, A Xiang suddenly pulled out a sharp blade and stabbed Jiang more than ten times in the left and right arms, legs, and back. He then fled. Jiang was usually strong, and after being injured, he ran to his friend Xu Fugen, 29 years old, a native of Wuxi, who lived in a flat house in Kangjiazhai, Fulili Road, and asked him to send him to the hospital for treatment immediately. Xu hired a car and sent him to Guangci Hospital, but he died at 12:00 p.m. due to excessive bleeding from the wounds. The hospital reported to the French Patrol Room, which sent detectives to investigate and sent the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch for autopsy, and notified Jiang Bai, the wife of the deceased, to come to the case. Yesterday morning, a report was made to the Special Court, and Chief Prosecutor Qiao Wanxuan and forensic medical officers, etc., arrived at the place at noon to verify that the deceased had died from knife wounds sustained before death. After questioning the deceased's wife and witness Xu Fugen, he ordered the deceased's wife, Jiang Bai, to claim the body, and the murderer was to be arrested by the Xiangwu Office.

Unable to Endure Debt Pressure, Chen Xuebao Dies by Poison, His Brother Reports to the Police, Huang Shushen and Others Detained 141

Chen Xuebao, a native of Huai'an, (48 years old), lived on Zhonghua Xin Road, Pushan Road, Zhabei, and worked at the Fuxin Factory to make a living. His wife had passed away. Last year, through a friend Dai Rong, he married Ms. Li from Ningbo as his second wife. Chen Xuebao was in financial straits, so he asked his friend Gao San to borrow 15 yuan from Huang Shushen, using his work badge as collateral (monthly interest of 2 yuan). Unexpectedly, Ms. Li had not been married long before she returned to Ningbo on the pretext of going home, and swept away the household items and clothing, never to return. After Chen searched everywhere, there was no trace of her. It was like releasing a pigeon without return, and he lost both his person and his money. He spent his days sighing in frustration and had no heart to work, which led to his situation becoming increasingly difficult. Recently, the creditor Huang Shushen asked Chen Xuebao to pay back the debt. Chen had no way to pay, so he sold six piglets raised in his house and obtained 21 yuan, which he paid back in full. Huang Shushen believed that Chen Xuebao owed 24 yuan in principal and interest, and still owed 3 yuan, and refused to return the factory badge that Chen had mortgaged. Chen Xuebao was anxious and went to the factory foreman Yu Shaotang for help. Yu not only refused to help, but also helped Huang Shushen extort payment, otherwise he would stop Chen from working forever. Chen Xuebao was extremely worried upon hearing this. Because his house was bare and he could not work, he felt that life was worse than death, so he secretly took poison and died the day before yesterday. After his brother Chen Xueru found out, he reported the information to the Xinzha Branch, which ordered the police to detain Huang Shushen, Dai Rong, Yu Shaotang, and others and send them to the Public Security Bureau. At the same time, he ordered the local guarantor Wang Shaoting to report to the local court for an autopsy. Zhang Zi, the prosecutor commissioned by the court, and Shen Qixiu, the autopsy officer, *were present. Chen Xuebao's autopsy confirmed that he had died from taking poison. A form was filled out, and it was ruled that the family could claim the coffin. The defendants will be sent to court for interrogation.

Chinese Compradore of British Public Bus Company, Song Zi'ang Confesses to Embezzling Public Funds, Due to Failed Speculation, Misappropriated More Than 70,000 Gold Yuan, Police Press Charges of Occupational Embezzlement 142

The Chinese compradore of the British-owned China General Omnibus Company was originally Song Lifeng, a native of Chuansha, Pudong. All the company's accounts for salaries and expenses of employees were under his management. In 1929, Zhu Lifeng was transferred to the position of General Manager of the Hankou First Yarn Factory of the British-owned Anli Foreign Firm. The vacancy left by the General Omnibus Company was filled by Zhu Lifeng's cousin Song Zi'ang (formerly an employee in the compradore's office). Song Zi'ang usually handled affairs quite well, so he was deeply trusted by the authorities. However, since last year, Song Zi'ang suddenly engaged in speculative businesses and suffered repeated losses, amounting to more than 100,000 yuan. Even all his property, such as shares in the Baoda Qianzhuang at No. 15 Shandong Road, was not enough to pay off his debts. The creditors continued to press for payment, and Song was unable to cope. He sold the copper coins stored in the warehouse at No. 1171 Kangnao Road for approximately 92,000 yuan in national currency, and embezzled more than 10,000 yuan in company salaries issued to employees. In total, the amount of embezzlement reached 73,759 yuan and 73 cents. Song knew that this matter could not be concealed in the end, so at 8:45 a.m. the day before yesterday, he went to the General Patrol Room with lawyer Yu Xiangqin to surrender himself. After investigation by West Detective Ha Hui and Chinese Detective, Song Zi'ang was detained. Yesterday morning, the Patrol Room lawyer Wang* Tang explained the situation to the First Special District Court Criminal Court, stating that according to the defendant's confession, the total amount of embezzlement was 73,759 yuan and 73 cents, but according to the number issued by the General Omnibus Company, it was 76,666 yuan and 69 cents. The Patrol Room is now prosecuting the case according to Article 336, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law for the crime of occupational embezzlement and requesting a judgment according to the law. The General Omnibus Company also commissioned lawyer Fan Gang to appear in court and file a civil suit. The company's representative Gao Ersiden also went to court to explain the accounts. The Patrol Room lawyer Wang also said that regarding the more than 50,000 yuan of copper coins, because the company learned that the central government was going to collect copper coins, it stored the copper coins from ticket sales over the past few months in wooden boxes in the warehouse, waiting for the price to rise before selling them. The defendant sold the copper coins to the qianzhuang one after another, so although the wooden boxes in the warehouse still exist, the copper coins inside have been sold. When questioned, Song Zi'ang confessed that he was 山 for failing in speculation and did not deny it. Lawyer Yu Xiangqin requested that the defendant be allowed to post bail so that he could go outside and negotiate with the plaintiff on a settlement method for the civil suit. The plaintiff's agent lawyer Fan Gang also agreed to this request. Judge Feng Shide ordered that the case be adjourned for another week. Zhu Zi'ang paid a 20,000 yuan shop guarantee and guaranteed to be present whenever summoned.

Zhou Exuan Sues Zhang Zhuying Again, The Relationship Between Him and Du Nan Has Been Established, Now Willing to Pay 15 Yuan per Month for Living Expenses 143

Zhou Exuan, the son of Zhou Weishi, a wealthy merchant from Suzhou who was traveling in Shanghai, favored a famous prostitute named Zhang Zhuying. After she became pregnant, he removed her name from the register and planned to place her in a concubine's room. When Weishi found out about this, he strictly ordered his son to break off relations with the prostitute. Exuan had to part with her and handed over the son, Du Nan, to Zhang for upbringing, with a monthly living allowance. Until the previous year, Zhang requested that Zhou increase the living expenses for the son from 50 yuan per month to 70 yuan, which was rejected by Zhou. The original amount was also stopped, so she accused Zhou of abandonment in the Xiyuan and sentenced him to six months in prison with a suspended sentence. After the case was finalized, Zhou hoped to avoid Zhang Zhuying representing her son to demand education expenses, so he filed a lawsuit against Zhang for the guardianship of Du Nan, requesting that Zhang hand over Du Nan to him for education and guardianship. However, after three trials, Zhou's lawsuit failed. Now Zhou has started anew, hired lawyer Huang Yi, and submitted another statement to the First Special District Court, saying that since his father-son relationship with Du Nan has been established, the living expenses of Du Nan should naturally be borne by him and is willing to give 15 yuan per month for support. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Dai Rongduo opened a court hearing. The defendant Zhang Zhuying and Du Nan commissioned lawyer Xiang Xun to appear in court. First, lawyer Huang stated the intention of the prosecution, saying that the plaintiff had sent a letter to the defendant in April stating the matter of giving 15 yuan per month to Du Nan for living expenses, but had not received a reply, so he filed a lawsuit. Then, lawyer Xiang raised a legal issue, saying that Zhang was Du Nan's guardian, and the plaintiff could only sue Du Nan, not include Zhang as a defendant. Lawyer Huang then amended the statement in court. Lawyer Xiang continued to say that the alimony given by Zhou Exuan was initially 50 yuan per month, and a lawsuit arose because Zhang requested an increase. Zhou has now filed this lawsuit again after losing several times, really fearing that Zhang will file a lawsuit against him in the name of guardian for a large amount of alimony. Therefore, this is a preemptive measure. The Zhou family has property of more than 10 million yuan and is only willing to give his own son a meager 15 yuan per month for living expenses, which does not seem reasonable. Lawyer Huang heard this and determined that the point of contention was the amount, so he asked the court to order the defendant to clearly state the amount they wanted for discussion. Judge Dai then ordered an adjournment for another hearing.

Fujian Native Association Expands Organization 148

The Fujian Native Association in Shanghai has recently been actively reorganizing its affairs and expanding its membership. Several meetings have already been held. The second special committee meeting was held the other day, attended by Jiang Yinan, Chi Yunfei, Song Yuanyuan, Ye Gengfu, Xie Denan, Zhuang Dingdong, Chen Shaohua, Lin Shengqin, Chen Shuo, Shangguan Shufen, Huang Renfang, Yang Menglin, Huang Jianzhong, and dozens of others. Song Yuanyuan chaired the meeting, with Zheng Yunqing as the recorder. The chairman reported on the resolutions of the previous meeting and stated that the participants in this special committee were all leaders from various sectors, which was a very positive sign. There are nearly 100,000 Fujian natives in Shanghai. Whether the organization of the Native Association is sound has a significant bearing on the vital interests of each fellow native. It is hoped that fellow natives will participate in unison to seek unity and promote the spirit of self-governance. Subsequently, the drafting committee reported on several draft amendments to the association's charter. The main provision, Article 3, stipulates duties that are of great importance and is therefore reproduced below: A. To promote education, charity, health, and other related undertakings. B. To safeguard the industries of all members and promote economic mutual assistance. C. To pay attention to the livelihoods of all members and find ways to introduce them to employment. D. To raise scholarships to reward members for advanced academic studies. E. To help plan and save on expenses for the consumption of all members in terms of clothing, food, housing, transportation, medical care, sanitation, weddings, funerals, lawsuits, entertainment, and other items. F. When members' public or private burdens are exceptionally exploited, to investigate and convey information or even request improvements on their behalf. G. To provide impartial mediation when disputes arise between members or with other parties, or to request government offices to resolve them promptly on their behalf. H. To pay attention to the province's reform matters and present opinions to the government at any time, but matters concerning individuals should be resolved by a general meeting of basic members. I. To accept requests from fellow natives coming to and from Shanghai for guidance or publicity and introduction. J. To accept the entrustment of fellow natives at home and abroad, to handle or contact and investigate various matters on their behalf. It was also resolved to solicit members. Chen Shuo was specially recommended to draft a brief introduction and formulate implementation methods, and Li Dingxin, Chen Jiliang, Zhu Yuanyuan, Li Denghui, and Jiang Yinan were publicly elected as the presidium of five people. Many routine cases were also passed. The meeting adjourned at 6 o'clock.

House Collapse Injures People in Sanlintang 164

Cao Yongkun, a farmer from Pudong, 42 years old, married Ju, currently 40 years old. They lived in Wu's Jiagang in Sanlintang, Pudong, and made a living by farming and selling vegetables. Although their income was meager, they were diligent and thrifty, so the family lived a fairly comfortable life. They had built a flat in Wu's Jiagang for the whole family to live in. Unexpectedly, the building materials were not strong, and suddenly at 7:50 AM yesterday morning, with a sudden sound, the entire house collapsed. At that time, Cao and Ju were still fast asleep and had not gotten up, so they were both buried in the rubble and debris. Fortunately, nearby neighbors heard the sound and came to investigate. They invited strong men to turn the two over, but Cao's head and chest and Ju's head and both hands were all injured, and the injuries were quite serious. The neighbors then tried to send them to the Shanghai Municipal Hospital in Puxi for treatment.

Laundry Company Employee Drowns in River 165

At about 11:00 AM yesterday, the City Ferry operating the Chunbei-Huanbei route departed from the Chunjin Wharf in Pudong and headed to the opposite bank. Not far from the dock, a young man suddenly jumped into the river without anyone noticing and committed suicide. The captain immediately noticed and stopped the engine to rescue him, but the man had already sunk without a trace. A business card left by the deceased was found on the ship, printed with the words "Paramount Laundry Company." A staff member was sent to the Paramount Company on Lafayette Road, French Concession, to inquire, and it was learned that the deceased was indeed an employee of the company, named Zheng Meisheng, 20 years old, from Ningbo. On the morning of the 7th of this month, because he lost an expensive piece of clothing from a Westerner, he was afraid of being blamed by the store and left privately, unexpectedly taking this extreme measure. The deceased was wearing an Ai Guo cloth shirt and pants, with long hair.

Central Bank Inspection Report 170

The 286th inspection report on the Central Bank's issuance reserve for convertible banknotes states: In accordance with Article 13 of the Central Bank Law, this committee is responsible for inspecting the amount of convertible banknotes issued by the bank and the reserve funds. The 286th inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of the bank on June 6, 1936. The results of the inspection are reported as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible banknotes issued is 294,316,310 silver dollars, including 264,473,785 silver dollar notes and 29,842,525 subsidiary currency notes. The total amount of the convertible banknote reserve is 294,316,310 silver dollars, including 199,836,210 silver dollars in cash reserve. This cash reserve is stored in the bank's issuing headquarters, branches, and sub-branches at 143,128,282.71 silver dollars and with other banks at 56,700,792.29 silver dollars. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 94,480,100 silver dollars. (B) The total amount of Customs Gold Unit (CGU) convertible banknotes issued is 373,324.7 CGU. The total amount of the CGU convertible banknote reserve is 373,324.7 CGU. This reserve includes 7,351.95 taels of standard gold, equivalent to 373,324.7 CGU at a fixed price of 5.0779. In accordance with Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve shall be at least 60%, and the remainder shall be guaranteed by legal guarantees. The results of this inspection show that the current reserve exceeds 60%, and the guarantee reserve is within 40%, which is in compliance with the regulations. This report is hereby issued on June 8, 1936, by Li Fusun, Chairman of the Supervisory Board of the Central Bank; Supervisors Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, and Xu Jili.

### North China Daily News Editorial - A Frank Discussion of Recent Changes in the Southwest - Titled "Tragedy or Farce?" - Shaking the Foundation of the Country Invites a Bad Reputation 180

The Shen Shi News Agency translated the North China Daily News editorial on the 9th: The development of events in Guangzhou in recent days is truly an ominous phenomenon for China. Chen Jitang's boastful declaration and the telegrams from Chen and Li Zongren to various parties can be taken as an expression of their true intentions, or as meaningless things. If these things are meaningless, then this is their irresponsibility, and as a result, China suffers a major loss. In recent months, the world has paid unusual attention to the China issue. The central government's active economic construction and the spirit of manly self-help shown in dealing with Sino-Japanese issues have been well received in all quarters. Chiang Kai-shek's insightful patience with the Kwantung Army's invasion of North China, and Zhang Qun's appointment as Minister of Foreign Affairs, also indicate the importance of negotiating with Japan. The central government knows the danger of abandoning a compromise attitude, and local governments, no matter how independent they are, should not rashly oppose the central government, because its geographical relationship absolutely cannot make its opposition effective, but puts those close to the conflict line in an extremely difficult position. Therefore, the only effect of the recent declarations from Guangdong is to destroy China's moral credibility. They obliterated the central government's painstaking tolerance of the Southwest Political Affairs Committee, and at a time when the crisis is saturated, they intend to shake the foundation of China's national policy. They clearly want to use counterfeit patriotism to invite a bad reputation and cause the danger of subversion. If the generals of Guangdong and Guangxi sincerely want to open the army to the north to resist the Japanese invasion, how dare they ask how they can reach the Yangtze River basin? Li Zongren has many Japanese military advisers under his command, and they should understand a little military common sense to accomplish the purpose he claims. If the central government accepts his suggestion and allows him to have the convenience of realizing this interesting war, is he truly eager to accept this opportunity? He knows - everyone knows - he is not willing to accept it. However, observing this problem cannot be so simple. The central government's negotiations with Tokyo have fallen into an extremely difficult situation. Although it can tolerate the Southwest's division of power in internal affairs, it cannot abandon its responsibilities because of its interference. Therefore, if the Southwest continues to adopt a provocative attitude towards Japan, I am afraid that before long, the central government will be blamed by the Japanese. At that time, the means taken by the Japanese soldiers, who are full of aggressive meaning and have made precise plans, will be more serious than what the Southwest is now showing. The leader of Guangdong said, "United Front against Japan." This sentence also failed to move people much, because he put the cart before the horse. A "united front" can be said to be the prelude to the completion of the military plan, and there must be a certainty and necessity to complete this military plan first. Now, because of the need to unite the front, first there is a local military movement. Isn't this self-contradictory? The Southwest leaders claim that they do not want to cause a civil war and that they want to urge the central government to fight against Japan. They should know that these two reasons are illogical side by side. It should be known that urging the government with theory and public opinion is one thing, and mobilizing troops to invade neighboring provinces to achieve their goals is another thing. What kind of impression will this development have on the Japanese? It is difficult to predict. If the two parties have different political views and discuss their differences under the supervision of the people, then the result of such a discussion, which is free from the threat of direct action, can take accurate steps to preserve the interests of the country. Once the dark clouds of contention are cleared, the country can gain great benefits. The telegram from the Southwest Political Affairs Committee says, "If the current situation is allowed to continue, the enemy's ambitions will never be satisfied." However, we should know that domestic armed warfare gives the enemy the best opportunity to satisfy its ambitions. If China is truly in crisis, then last week's developments have further aggravated this crisis. We sincerely hope that even now, the two sides in China with different political views can accept wise advice, so as to stop the performance of this farce and avoid the final tragedy.

Shanghai's Silk Weaving and Embroidery Industry (No. 27 of the General Situation of Shanghai Industry and Commerce) Compiled by China Credit Information 181

Overview

The embroidery industry is one of China's fine art crafts and occupies a considerable position in women's handicrafts. Tracing its origins, it dates back to four thousand years ago. The fu and fu of the Tang and Yu dynasties were the origins of the embroidery industry. However, from the Tang and Yu dynasties to modern times, it was only limited to the formal attire of the royal family and the official uniforms of civil and military officials, so the industry never had room for vigorous development.

After China opened up to overseas trade in the late Ming Dynasty, Portuguese people purchased Chinese embroidery pieces and brought them back to their country. The king greatly appreciated them, and from then on, Chinese embroidery gradually gained a reputation overseas, and Chinese people also began to pay attention to it, and the industry began to have the opportunity to gradually stand out. Since the Qing Dynasty, culture and art have progressed with each passing day, and efforts have been made to promote embroidery. In addition to royal tributes and formal attire such as python robes, shawls, and mandarin squares, other daily clothing was also prepared, and the business was booming. The annual consumption value was more than ten million taels of silver, which was the golden age of the industry.

Since the Republic of China, the clothing system has changed, and the machinery of European and American countries has evolved, and new products have emerged one after another. Clothing is generally replaced by machine-made products, and the embroidery industry has gradually declined, gradually entering a state of depression. After the tenth year of the Republic of China, the industry opened up a new path, changing embroidery products into fine art decorations and using them as gifts for relatives and friends. At that time, the social economy was still relatively prosperous, and the purchasing power was strong, so the business could be maintained. Since the twentieth year of the Republic of China, due to the frequent years of natural and man-made disasters in various parts of the country, coupled with the loss of the Northeast and the end of the Shanghai War, domestic industry and commerce were exhausted, and the economic panic became increasingly profound. Therefore, the business declined greatly. According to people in the industry, the industry's annual turnover in recent years has decreased by 70% to 80% compared with the prosperous period. The general situation of the industry is described below:

Types of Embroidery Products Embroidery is a famous ancient craft in China. According to its embroidery methods, it can be roughly divided into two types: one is called straight-grain embroidery, which is arranged by the method of reciprocating warp and weft; the other is called short-needle embroidery, which is accumulated by the method of five-down knotting. Straight-grain embroidery: originates from Weiting Town, Kunshan, Jiangsu Province, and is woven with colored silk warp and weft, and is called kesi, but it is rare in the market now. Short-needle embroidery is divided into Guangdong embroidery and Suzhou embroidery. Suzhou embroidery is also known as Gu embroidery, because the embroidery of figures was created by the concubine of Gu Huihai of Shanghai, who was good at needlework and embroidery. The embroidered figures are lifelike, the characters are also methodical, the embroidery products are exquisite, and the value is the most expensive, which is what is called painting embroidery. However, the Gu family has no descendants who can make it. Today, Hunan's Xiang embroidery is actually above Guangdong embroidery and Suzhou embroidery, because Xiang embroidery focuses on realism. All embroidered flowers, birds, fish, and insects are vivid and lifelike, but the needles used are too thick, which can be seen from a distance but not up close, and the price is expensive and the output is not much.

In recent years, in addition to the above-mentioned types, there are also Wenzhou embroidery, Saixiu embroidery, and silk woven brocade embroidery. The Wenzhou embroidery handicraft group is inferior, and the paintings are too clumsy, which often leads to drawing a tiger like a dog, which is difficult to compete with Suzhou embroidery and Xiang embroidery. Even illiterate people regard it as Gu embroidery. Saixiu embroidery is completely painted according to the paintings with gelatinous pigments. The products are still pleasing to the eye, but they are lifeless, and the gelatin is easy to fall off, so it is not durable.

Silk woven brocade embroidery was created in the tenth year of the Republic of China by Mr. Du Jinsheng of Hangzhou, Zhejiang. He is well-versed in machine-woven fabrics and has a lot of experience. In view of the backwardness of domestic art and crafts and sticking to old methods, he resolutely adopted the organization of straight-grain embroidery, improved it, and used new machinery for precision preparation. It is divided into two types: colored and plain. The products are fast, and there are many colors. All hand-embroidered items can be woven, and the colors are bright and appropriate, and the expressions are lifelike, and it is no different from the living at first glance. It can be said that it is unique in the embroidery industry.

Uses of Embroidery Products Since there are so many types of embroidery products as mentioned above, the most widely used is Suzhou embroidery, because its products are finely stitched and suitable for tailoring quilt covers, tablecloths, embroidered pillows, embroidered cushions, and other brocade embroidery clothing materials. The items are both gorgeous and practical, and the sales are quite wide. As for other embroidered items, they are generally fine art decorations, mainly featuring famous paintings and calligraphy, landscapes, and figures, followed by curtains, table skirts, and seat cushions. Except for Xiang embroidery and brocade embroidery, each has its own special advantages, and the sales are smooth. The rest are mediocre, and they are not as good as Suzhou embroidery.

Market Price of Embroidery Products Since embroidery is one of the art crafts, its price is not fixed, which is by no means comparable to machine-made products. The embroidery work is slow, and the output is not much, so it is often one to several times higher than machine-made products. In addition to the above-mentioned reasons, embroidery also depends on the quality of the satin material, the size of the embroidery piece, the complexity of the pattern, and the density of the needlework. According to the industry's heyday, calculated by fixed pieces, it was as high as thousands of hundreds of yuan, medium to three or five hundred yuan, and less than one hundred yuan or so. Ordinary finished products range from three or several yuan to several hundred yuan. However, in recent years, times have changed, the business has declined miserably, and the market price has fallen sharply, at least 30% to 40% less than in the past. As for the wholesale selection of embroidery products, the wholesale price is particularly cheap, and the transaction can be concluded at about 50% off the listed price. It is said that the profit is still very rich, because the embroidery work is cheap (from three or four corners to hundreds of yuan per piece), and the cost is relatively small, which is not easy for non-industry people to see clearly. It is said that in the 20th year of the Republic of China, this port's Jinhua Yao Xiang Embroidery Shop undertook to embroider a photo of US President Hoover, about three inches square, and the plain price was 1,000 yuan in national currency, which was still considered cheap. Later, it won an art award from the Chicago Exposition in the United States to show its appreciation.

Silk woven brocade embroidery is made by machines, the output is fast, the output is large, and it can be increased or decreased at any time according to market needs. The price of the products, whether they are custom-made or spot goods, is calculated according to the size and complexity of the structure (but the custom-made ones are subject to a plate-making fee). The price starts from 3 corners for 3×4 inches to 80 yuan for 39×80 inches, and there will be no increase or decrease in the future, which is more than twice as cheap as embroidery, so the business is quite developed, and it is by no means fluke to be able to keep pace with embroidery products. In recent years, affected by the economic depression, the purchasing power is weak, and the business has plummeted. If there are wholesale transactions, it is willing to sell at 50% off the listed price. (To be continued)

Shenbao National Goods Special Issue

Words of Contribution

Smuggling and Reporting by the Same Industry 182

— Yang'an

National goods and smuggling stand in irreconcilable positions. With smuggling, there are no national goods. To protect national goods is to eliminate smuggling. There is nothing in life that cannot be done, no industry that cannot be engaged in, no place where money cannot be made, but one must engage in this smuggling life. These are either people who do not know human shame or madmen.

Eliminating smuggling and using secret reports is indeed very effective. But the most effective method is to borrow the power of the same industry association and give it full power to inspect and report. Then, all industries will be under martial law, and they will supervise each other. The trend of smuggling may be curbed. Therefore, the most important method is to strengthen the organization of the same industry association, so that each industry association has real strength and a consistent attitude to deal with smugglers. The call for amending the same industry association laws is now a nationwide trend. Reforming the laissez-faire doctrine and replacing it with interventionism is the key element of amending this law. Mr. Hu Xiyuan's proposal to organize an industrial association and a chamber of commerce as legitimate groups of industry and commerce is also to strengthen the power of industrial groups. The fundamental solution is indeed a unique view. It is heard that various groups are assigning members to study in order to submit a memorial to the central government for adoption and implementation. Recently, the Electrical Machinery and Silk Weaving Industry Association, the Silk and Satin Industry Association, and the Rayon Industry Association jointly decided that rayon packages in each factory must be affixed with stamps. If not, they will be regarded as smuggled goods. It is heard that everyone has unanimously agreed. If each industry association has this kind of control power, then smuggling is not to be feared.

Extraordinary Times and Saving the Country with National Goods 183

— Meng Zhao

Recently, economic experts and political figures often publish financial fallacies in extraordinary times, emergency financial measures, and planned financial management. They are eloquent and indeed, the country is in a very dangerous environment! Experts' theories are not only eloquent, but also plans that should be in place in extraordinary times. Let's take a look at the smuggling problem in the North, which is already extremely serious! According to reports, the Tianjin Customs statistics show that the customs and tax cards of the Great Wall collected a total of 41 million yuan in taxes last year. This year, due to the impact of smuggling, the reduction reached as much as 20 million yuan! Although the export tax increased by several hundred thousand yuan, it is far from enough to offset it. And someone pointed out that our Tianjin, Qinhuangdao, and Zhifu customs armed gunboats were cracking down on smuggling in the Bohai Bay, accusing us of invading public territorial waters and protesting to us... Their unreasonable demands, the evil forces of economic aggression; the conspiracy to dominate our country's entire finances; and the complex background of serious smuggling have all been clearly revealed!

From extraordinary times, I also thought of saving the country with national goods. Chinese people using Chinese goods is a matter of course. No matter how cheap a certain product is! Especially smuggled goods! We must not pay attention to it, and we must not be tempted! We must know that the country can only use national goods for one day if it survives. If the country is destroyed and the family is destroyed, our clothing, food, and supplies will be controlled by the enemy. If we want to buy national goods with all our heart and want to save the country with all our heart, it may be too late! Therefore, I say that the arrival of extraordinary times is the day when the Chinese people unite and step up the implementation of "saving the country with national goods"! We must not neglect it for a moment!

A Record of Visiting the China Educational Supplies Factory 184

— Quan Jia

The day before yesterday morning, it was very hot. We took the opportunity of the week to visit our teacher, Mr. Ling Wenzhi, on Kunming Road, and by the way, we visited the China Educational Supplies Factory where he works. Although it was about to snow, we didn't feel cold at all.

The factory is divided into three major workshops: the first workshop is divided into five departments: metalworking, woodworking, painting, electroplating, and assembly. Inside, they probably manufacture scientific instruments and other supplies. Many schools use them and all agree that they are satisfactory. In the past, all kinds of instruments relied on imported goods, but now most of them can be replaced by domestic products.

The second workshop is for making globes, human models, specimens, and microscope slides. Mr. Ling said, "The workers here not only have to work hard, but also have 'talent' and training. It often takes several weeks to complete a specimen. For example, the fish anatomy model, the first step is to carefully dissect it, and the second step is to understand the fish's organization and explain it clearly. Many people who lack this kind of 'talent' will never succeed. A fish is not expensive, but after dissection, it will cost a lot of money." Many people who make human models use thick cardboard to make human shapes, big and small, male and female, which is very interesting. Making this work also requires several steps. Some parts are made of thick paper, and some parts are made of plaster. After assembling, the colors must be painted. The workers must understand the human physiological organization. We also went to the microscope slide department and saw many glass slides with various shapes of germs inside. These peculiar tools will integrate "learning" and "facts", and the function is very great. The preparation of specimens can be divided into four parts: soaking, drying, skeletons, and peeling. After watching for a while, we went to the third workshop.

This workshop only makes monthly, daily, weekly, and hourly clocks. China is still the first manufacturer. With this clock, you only need to turn the spring, and it will automatically report the date and time. For example, on the day we visited, the left corner of the clock was marked with the month, day, and day of the week. This clock has many conveniences. There are five procedures for making clocks: the first part is to make a sample. After the sample is made, the metalworking department doubles the metal products according to the sample, such as gears, shafts, needles, and other parts. The third is the mold-making department, which makes the outline of the clock, and then sends it to the installation department for installation. After the installation is completed, the factory will also test it in the testing department to ensure its accuracy. In this way, the clock is completed. Except for springs and other things that China absolutely does not produce, most of the rest are made of domestic products, so that money will not flow to foreign countries.

Finally, Mr. Ling invited us to the showroom, where various products are displayed, from kindergarten to university, all very complete. To the east of the factory is a botanical and zoological garden for cultivating the factory's use in making specimens. Recently, it will pay attention to three items: scout supplies, children's toys, and economic instruments. All products of the factory are sold by the Zhonghua Book Company, and the total turnover is more than 500,000 yuan per year.

Finally, we were very grateful to Mr. Ling for his warm reception. This visit increased our knowledge a lot and we were extremely satisfied.

Lu Zhongwen and Ye Liang Invented a Rotary Three-Way Light Bulb 185

— Dai

This is certainly a gratifying thing. After the prelude to 1936 unfolded, we heard about people inventing things one after another. Who said that the Chinese have no inventing power? Now everyone doesn't believe it. Recently, we learned that in Nanhui, not far from Shanghai, two young people, Lu Zhongwen and Ye Liang, invented a rotary three-way light bulb. This is certainly good news in the promotion of national goods!

In recent years, Chinese people have set up factories to manufacture light bulbs themselves. There are also many so-called domestic light bulbs. However, most of the products are rough and cannot compete with imported goods. So what is the result? Until now, the light bulb business is still monopolized by foreign manufacturers. Now, Lu and Ye have invented a rotary three-way light bulb, and we deeply hope that it can defeat foreign light bulbs and make them disappear from the Chinese market.

It is said that this rotary three-way light bulb is divided into two types, A and B. Type A has three tungsten filaments of different brightness, manufactured in one light bulb, such as 50 watts, 25 watts, and 5 watts. If you need any light, you only need to rotate the outer ring above the bulb head slightly to change it. Moreover, when one brightness is lit, the other two tungsten filaments are completely off, so use a small light when there is nothing to do, a medium light when working, and a large light for banquets. One light bulb has three changes, and it is extraordinarily convenient to change it as you like.

Type B is a light bulb with three tungsten filaments of the same brightness. In this way, after your light bulb burns out one after a period of time, you can use the remaining two. You only need to rotate it until all three tungsten filaments are completely burned out before it becomes waste.

Therefore, in fact, types A and B light bulbs, although they are one light bulb, have three light bulb uses, and this three-way light bulb saves electricity, is easy to use, and will never explode or bump. The bulb head can automatically turn on and off. You only need to rotate the bulb slightly to turn it on or off. There is no need to use a separate switch. The chrome-plated appearance is also very beautiful. Therefore, once it is shipped in the future, it is very suitable for shops, schools, and public and private institutions.

Lu Zhongwen and Ye Liang are both graduates of the Municipal People's Livelihood Middle School. After leaving school, they worked for an electrical appliance company, so they have a good understanding of electrical appliances. This was invented after more than a year of research. Now the Ministry of Industry has expressed its commendation and has granted a special patent for five years. Lu and Ye are also actively preparing and widely soliciting shares, and the establishment of a factory is not far away.

It is said that the opening of this light bulb factory requires a capital of at least 20,000 yuan. Only half of it has been raised. Once the capital is sufficient, it will start manufacturing. If the shares can be raised to 100,000 yuan or 80,000 yuan, then it can be manufactured on a large scale. Their factory name has been determined as "Central Three-Way Light Bulb Factory", and the factory site is planned to be selected in the Xiaoshadu area. All preparations are being actively carried out. It is deeply hoped that domestic capitalists will actively invest so that the careers of these two young people can be successful one day.

Communication

Mr. Jiang Yunshan Talks About National Goods in the Japanese Market 186

— Xu Youwen

In the middle of last month, I went to Tokyo for private affairs. I was invited by Mr. Jiang Yunshan to have lunch at Meguro Gajoen. Mr. Jiang has been in the East for many years and works in the Chinese restaurant of the garden. During the banquet, he told me the crux of why national goods cannot be sold well in Japan, and he was deeply saddened! I specially recorded Mr. Jiang's conversation to fill this publication, hoping that all readers will pay attention to it.

Reporter: Mr. Jiang, you must be very familiar with the trade situation of our national goods in the Japanese market, right?

Mr. Jiang: In the past, Japanese people often held special excellent concepts about our country's goods. This concept arose from the abundance of our country's products! On the one hand, the durability of the goods and the cheapness of the goods drove their procurement goals, thinking that Chinese goods were more noble than European and American products. Therefore, business trade was not stagnant. What is most noteworthy is that many Japanese people who like to drink tea and wine feel unnatural without a pot of Chinese wine and Chinese tea at the table. National goods also occupied a considerable position in the Japanese market.

Reporter: In this way, our country's goods are so popular in Japan, and the sales must be wide. Why has the amount of exports to Japan been decreasing day by day in recent years, resulting in the lifelessness that is currently dying?

Mr. Jiang: Those who engage in international trade are disorganized and lack control, and the government also lacks advisers, allowing them to run rampant. You must know that engaging in international trade is not comparable to domestic transactions, and the procedures are not so simple. The most important principles of businessmen are credibility and integrity. The credibility and integrity of international traders also represent the credibility and integrity of the entire country's trade! The reason why our country's goods were popular with the Japanese in the past was because they were so-called cheap and good. In recent years, because businessmen have been greedy for small profits, they have turned the goods upside down. In this way, credibility has been lost. Even if it is a real beauty, who will believe it? In the past, there were many Chinese goods in Gajoen. Those Japanese people only needed Chinese goods, and they did not care about the high price. Therefore, sales increased layer by layer, and Chinese goods in Gajoen were also pushed to the highest position. Now, the credibility of businessmen has been lost, and the position and credibility of the country's foreign trade have also been shaken! In Gajoen, no one cares about our country's goods anymore. The market is piled up in the corner. Even the business of the shops set up by overseas Chinese has suffered a setback!

Reporter: So, is the reason why our country's goods cannot occupy a considerable position in the Japanese market entirely due to the corruption and inferiority of businessmen's personalities?

Mr. Jiang: Isn't that right? I recall that when I first came to Japan, the most popular items in the Chinese restaurant of Gajoen were Huangjiu and Green Bean Shao, which were shipped from Shanghai. At that time, the Japanese aristocratic class, when they came to Gajoen, had to drink heavily to show their wealth. It can be imagined how high the price of wine was and how much the Japanese loved it! Later, businessmen wanted to make huge profits, so they diluted the wine with other kinds of water and mixed fish eyes with pearls, and raised the price, which led to a loss of credibility! Now, they have replaced it with famous European and American wines. It's the same here, and it's probably the same elsewhere! The breakdown of businessmen's personalities is the biggest blow to the country's foreign trade!

Reporter: I heard that the Japanese are paying attention to the raw materials and manufacturing methods of our country's products that are dumped to them everywhere. They are actively trying to imitate them, and mass-produce them to lower prices, so as to invisibly resist the dumping of our country's goods. Mr. Jiang, you have been in Japan for many years, and you must be very familiar with this, right?

Mr. Jiang: The fierce competition between the Japanese and our country's goods has indeed become irreconcilable.

World Games Track and Field Team Begins Training Today 188

Mr. Ma Yue Lun Addresses Team Yesterday, Fu Bao, Lu Wang, and He to Test Pole Vault on the 16th

The 15 members of the Chinese track and field team participating in the World Games, were announced the night before last. Regarding the pole vault event, the Track and Field Selection Committee has designated Fu Bao, Lu Wang, and He to test their results next Tuesday (the 16th) to select one person. Yesterday at 5 PM, Mr. John Ma gathered the representatives at the De Lin Apartments to give a speech. Liu Changchun was selected as the team captain on the spot, and Zhang Lingjia was selected as the liaison officer during the training period. The Chinese track and field team was officially established.

Team Members in Attendance

Those present at yesterday's meeting included Track and Field Selection Committee member Ma Yue Lun, team members Jian Changchun, Wang Shilin, Wang Zhengling, Chen Baoqiu, Guo Jie, Zhang Lingjia, Jia Lianren, Leng Peigen, Lin Shaozhou, Wu Bixian, Dai Shuguo, Huang Yingjie, Li Sen, and 13 others. Fu Jincheng and Cheng Jinguan were absent due to other engagements. Shen Kunnan, a coach, was also present.

Mr. Ma's Address

Around 5 PM, the team members arrived one after another. Mr. John Ma stood up and gave an address, briefly stating that all representatives of China attending the World Games should demonstrate the spirit of the Chinese nation. Since you all represent the country and the people, you must pay attention to your words, attitude, actions, clothing, and all details, and not take them lightly, so that various countries will have a good image of you in the international arena. During the training period, each representative must not be complacent because they have been selected, but must continue to work hard, break records, and improve their performance. Discipline should be strictly observed to avoid criticism from public opinion.

Reported Matters

After Mr. Ma finished his address, he made the following report: Training will begin on the 11th for a period of two weeks, from 4 PM to 6 PM, at Shen Garden. The training rules will be drafted by myself (Mr. Ma referred to himself), and after consulting with Mr. Song Junfu, the representatives will be notified. Tests will be conducted once a week. During the training period, you must return to your residence for rest after lunch every day, and are not allowed to go out before training. You must be in bed by 10 PM. During the training period, each person will receive a daily allowance of one dollar and 25 cents for meals and one dollar for miscellaneous expenses. During the training period, small-scale confrontations with various strong teams in the city will be arranged to increase competitive experience. The Association can handle leave matters for each representative's service unit and school. Passport photos can be taken at Wang's Photo Studio, and uniforms will be made by Wu Xingchang. All representatives will reside in the De Lin Apartments.

Election of Team Captain

After the report, Liu Changchun was elected as the team captain on the spot. Upon Mr. Liu's proposal, a liaison officer was chosen for the training period, and Zhang Lingjia was elected. Then, forms were filled out to obtain passports, and commemorative badges for the pre-selection confrontation, donated by the Association, were distributed. The meeting adjourned around 6 PM. After the meeting, the representatives went to have their uniforms made. It is said that the training instructors are Ma Yue Lun, Song Junfu, Shen Kunnan, Xia Xiang, and Shu Hong.

Training Methods

According to Mr. Ma, the training method will adopt individual training. Each day, group exercises will be done first to warm up the body, and then each person will practice their own event. I will be present at each individual training session to instruct the athletes on all postures and methods, and I will ask Song Junfu and Xia Xiang, the track and field team managers, to assist. Regarding the training policy, I advocate the inductive method, to enlighten and encourage each athlete's talent and ability to make progress, so that they can easily exert their inherent potential. I do not advocate the oppressive method. Mr. Ma finally said that the selection was increased from 12 to 16 people purely to send more representatives to observe sports, so that they would have more opportunities to seek future development. Regarding funding, efforts will still be made to raise it.

Random Notes of Our National World Games Football Team on Their European Tour 190

— Written and Sent by Li Huitang

Moving to Bandung

On May 18th at 10 AM, our entire team took the train to Bandung. Huitang and Dr. Rong stayed behind to handle public and private matters, and then took a car with friends at 3 PM, arriving in the evening. Bandung is a small city in the middle of densely packed mountains, about 160 kilometers from Batavia. It is known as the "Little Paris of the East." The weather is spring-like all year round, making it a very suitable place to live. I heard that after our team arrived, they were warmly welcomed by the local overseas Chinese community. In the afternoon, a general meeting was held, and Coach Yan gave a speech to express his gratitude. Our team is staying at the "Hequn" Hotel Union. After being in the hot and depressing Batavia, everyone felt comfortable and happy in the cool Bandung. However, the water there is particularly cold, and most people dare not bathe after dusk. Even if they do, they shiver and tremble in the tropical region of Southeast Asia, daring not to take a cold bath. Those who do not know the reason will definitely find it strange. In fact, there are many small cities in Southeast Asia located in valleys thousands of feet above sea level, which are most suitable for escaping the heat and recuperating. The weather is very similar to the cool autumn of our country. It is not surprising that people dare not take cold baths. After a good night's sleep, even a single blanket is not warm enough. On the 19th, we made contact with the Bandung selection team. Because they have the advantage of the terrain, they are known as the "local snakes." We ended up with a tie after a hard fight.

Record of the Bandung Match

May 19th was the date of our team's second match in Java. The opponent was the Bandung selection team, which had lost to the Batavia selection team by a score of 3 to 1 in the inter-city competition last week. We arrived at the stadium at 4 PM. First, the Party anthem and the Dutch national anthem were played, and then the Minister of the Army performed the opening ceremony. The result was a 2-2 tie. Huitang and Jiang Bai each scored one goal. Our lineup was as follows:

After the start of the match, our team launched wave after wave of attacks, but retreated again and again due to offside. The opponent's skills were extremely rough, but they were good at sprinting and using long passes to advance. Our defense was repeatedly trapped, and the field was uneven and the ground was as hard as iron, making the ball difficult to control. As a result, the opponent took advantage of the terrain and gained the upper hand. After 25 minutes, the opponent's goalkeeper committed a foul, and Huitang scored a penalty kick. Before long, our defense was slightly negligent, and the enemy center forward retaliated. The first half ended in a draw. After the break, we responded with a new formation.

Not long after taking the field, our team launched several fierce attacks, but they were all saved by their goalkeeper. After attacking for a long time without success, there was bound to be a mistake. Sure enough, after 15 minutes, the enemy had a sharp forward who seized the opportunity to score a goal. Our team first won and then drew, and then almost lost. With little time left, we poured all our strength into offense, transferring Jiang Bai to the front line to assist in the attack, adopting a "do or die" strategy. Unfortunately, the ball often bounced erratically, and although there were many opportunities, we often missed at the last moment. With only five minutes left before the end of the match, in the midst of dwindling hope, Jiang Bai finally managed to create a tie. Then, Bei Hua headed in a goal, but it was ruled out of bounds by the referee and did not count. The final whistle blew, and the match ended in a 2-2 tie. According to reports, although our team lost many opportunities that day due to unfamiliarity with the field and the inability to control the ball, the entire team was unusually disorganized, and the performance was lackluster. There was no way to deny it. The audience was dissatisfied, which was not surprising. After the match, the Minister of the Army awarded two silver cups, and Mr. Chen Baoshan, Huitang's childhood teacher, presented an embroidered flag on behalf of the Confucian group. Huitang accepted them separately, expressed his gratitude, and the crowd dispersed with cheers.

Education News

National Language Council Broadcast: Phonetic Symbols Class Starts Today 198

School Teachers, Normal Students, and Others Are Required to Attend, Divided into Elementary, Middle, and Advanced Levels, the Course Lasts Nine Weeks

The National Mandarin Education Promotion Association, in order to comply with the Ministry of Education's order to implement phonetic Chinese characters on July 1st of this year, and to stipulate that elementary schools and public schools first teach phonetic symbols, has specially opened a phonetic symbol broadcast training class, in order to train a large number of teachers. It has been launched in Shanghai first. The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education has issued a notice to all municipal and private elementary school Chinese teachers, public literacy school teachers, and normal school students to participate in the study. The association has been lecturing at the Shanghai Buddhist Sound Radio Station starting at 4:15 PM on June 8th. The details are recorded below:

Course Arrangement

The association divides phonetic symbols into elementary, middle, and advanced levels, and compiles a textbook for each level. The training period is a total of nine weeks. The elementary course focuses on basic practice of initials, finals, combined finals, and tones, lasting two weeks. The intermediate course focuses on pinyin practice and tone practice, lasting three weeks. This session has been shortened because it is too close to the summer vacation, and has been changed to two weeks, but the time for each session will be extended by 15 minutes to make up for the original time. The advanced course focuses on the pronunciation of retroflex finals, changes in tones, and flexible use of phonetics, lasting four weeks. The advanced level will not be offered temporarily this year. Because the advanced course must reach a considerable level of ability in the elementary and middle courses before proceeding to the advanced course, otherwise "it will be like trying to draw a tiger but ending up with something resembling a dog."

Class Starts Today

The association first explained the broadcasting situation, listening and learning attention, and sound checks in detail for the past two days. The formal elementary course is scheduled to start at 4:15 PM today, starting from scratch according to the elementary phonetic symbol textbook. Ma Guoying will be the lecturer. Listeners can follow the book to learn on time. It is reported that the organizers of the association said that the courses at all levels are very heavy, and the lecture time is very short, so they hope that the listeners will listen on time every day and do not interrupt or be absent. A very short practice time is reserved during the lecture time. It is hoped that the listeners will take the opportunity to follow along and practice. If you only use your ears to listen and not your mouth to learn, it will be difficult to improve your skills and methods. After listening to the lecture every day, you must take some time to practice fully. If listeners have any questions, they can send them directly to the Buddhist Sound Radio Station, 418 Hede Road, Shanghai, so that they can be answered.

The Preparatory Office of the Chinese Economic Society to Hold a Meeting in Shanghai in Late September

The Chinese Economic Society is the earliest established academic economic organization in China. Since its establishment in the twelfth year of the Republic of China, there have been branches and offices, and the number of members has reached more than 800. Since the election of Li Zhaohuan and Ma Yinchu as president and vice president, they have made unremitting efforts to carry out the affairs of the society. In addition to the Nanjing and Guangzhou branches, which have been established one after another, it has also been decided that the annual meeting of this session will be held in Shanghai in late September, which will be prepared by the Shanghai branch. A meeting was held a few days ago to discuss all the ongoing matters. Pan Lun was appointed as the director-general, Zhou Zhongqian as the deputy director-general, Wu Xiaoyuan and Zhang Sichuan as the general affairs group officer, Cao Lishun as the documents group officer, Zhou Zhongqian and Li Yunliang as the reception group officers, Li Zhaohuan and Tang Qingzeng as the thesis group officers, and Ma Yinchu and Jin Guobao as the debate group officers. It is also heard that the scope of the thesis for this session has been set as "Economic Issues in Extraordinary Times" and "Financial Issues in Extraordinary Times," which will be communicated to all societies to prepare. In addition to the thesis, another special feature of this annual meeting is the holding of academic debates. The topic "Should China seek internal price stability or foreign exchange stability in implementing the new financial policy?" has been selected. Members of the Shanghai and Nanjing branches will separately determine the pros and cons, and each will compile two groups, each group consisting of three debaters and one reserve member. The selection of debate members is currently underway in the two branches. At that time, the battle of words will surely be a great discussion.

Ministry of Education to Hold Summer Workshop for Agricultural Vocational School Teachers at Zhongda University, from July 20th to August 23rd 202

(Nanjing, 9th) In order to improve the agricultural knowledge and skills of teachers in agricultural vocational schools, the Ministry of Education will hold a summer workshop for teachers in agricultural vocational schools at Central University from July 10th to August 23rd this summer. Teachers of agricultural subjects in public and private agricultural vocational schools in various provinces and cities will participate in the workshop. Regulations have been formulated and a list of topics has been issued to each department for compliance. The names, schools, and desired study groups of the participants from each province and city are to be listed and reported to the Ministry by the end of June. Participants must report to the capital before July 10th. The training subjects are divided into plant production and animal production. The fee includes a sightseeing fee of 10 yuan, which will be paid by the original provincial and municipal education administrative organs or schools. The cost of accommodation and other expenses will be borne by the Ministry of Education. Travel expenses will be subsidized by the original school as appropriate. Selection method: Each school shall select one to two full-time teachers (one for each subject), but schools that enroll double grades in each academic year may send one more person. After the completion of the training, the teachers will still serve in the original school.

Chen Lijian Speaks on Active Social Education (1) 211

Chen Lijian, Director of the Department of Social Education of the Ministry of Education, spoke on "Active Social Education" on the Central Broadcasting Station on the evening of the 7th. His speech is as follows:

The Meaning of Social Education

What is social education? To this day, there is no universally accepted definition. There are also many similar terms, such as mass education, adult education, popular education, extended education, remedial education, and people's education, which are often used interchangeably, making the situation very complicated. This lack of uniformity, in the eyes of a few, leads to varied discussions and tricks. In fact, this non-standardized situation is precisely the vitality and hope of social education. Why? We must know that the history of social education is very short. Its emergence is only in the last decade or so. The addition of the Department of Social Education to the Ministry of Education in our country began in the first year of the Republic of China. It is a new undertaking, and traditional education cannot help it much. It is still evolving and cannot be stereotyped or standardized. It is a newborn baby with infinite future. It is the newly rising sun, and its contribution to mankind is unpredictable. British adult education expert Peffer said, "To give an accurate definition of adult education, it is best to wait until the adult education undertaking is more developed, because only when the undertaking is developed can we determine the nature based on the facts." This is very true. During this ongoing period, defining social education is naturally not an easy task. However, for the sake of defining the scope of work and pointing out the goals of efforts, it seems best to have a definition. Based on this idea, I will give a temporary definition of social education.

In my opinion, "Social education is education outside of school, or non-formal education outside of the formal school system." This seems extremely simple, but it seems acceptable for temporary application. Why do I say that social education is education outside of school? This can be explained by the matters currently under the jurisdiction of the Department of Social Education of the Ministry of Education in our country. The Department of Social Education is divided into two sections:

The first section is in charge of the following matters: Matters concerning mass education; Matters concerning phonetic symbols and literacy movements; Matters concerning popular reading materials; Matters concerning popular lectures; Matters concerning remedial education; Matters concerning special education for the disabled and other disabilities; Matters concerning national calendars; Matters concerning the Ministry's library.

The second section is in charge of the following matters: Matters concerning mass education centers; Matters concerning museums; Matters concerning libraries; Matters concerning the preservation of documents and antiquities; Matters concerning beautification education; Matters concerning the improvement of customs and popular entertainment (parks, dramas, movies, folk songs, customs, etc.); Matters concerning public sports; Matters concerning the Central Education Center. These were the regulations a few years ago. Recently, educational broadcasting, film education, labor education, and special education have also been under the jurisdiction of the Department of Social Education.

After looking at the matters listed above, we can understand that these educational undertakings are all things that formal school education does not have time for. For example, taking the first item of the first section, matters concerning mass education, the number of uneducated adult citizens in our country accounts for 80% of the national population. However, formal schools do not provide an opportunity for older, uneducated citizens to receive supplementary education. Our school system does not include education for older, uneducated citizens. All of the items listed above are very important and must be done. Now that schools do not pay attention to them, we naturally have to find other ways outside of school. This kind of educational facility outside of school is social education. (To be continued)

Finance - Pure Gold Soars - Call Loans Firm on the Market 212

Sellers Seize the Opportunity to Act: Resulting in Only Seventy Cents

The gold market was quite brisk yesterday due to the surge in pure gold. Unexpectedly, after the sellers seized the opportunity to act at high prices, the buyers suddenly became onlookers. Banks also held back and gradually lowered prices. In the end, it was still stable. In the early morning, overseas silver markets showed that London rose and the US was flat. The forward silver price in Montelieu fell by eight mils and rose by one cent. Exchange rates uniformly contracted. London raw gold rose by seven pence. The off-market tentative transaction opened higher at forty-four yuan. Although Fuxingyong made advances, Dadecheng, Yicheng, Yuanfengyong, and others unloaded, retreating to two and a half yuan. The Central Bank's posted rates were announced, with both the UK and the US flat. The customs gold unit rose by seven mils. The standard call loan price was posted higher at 1,133 yuan. The morning opening was still high. After the opening, the market was still stable, but due to pressure from major players taking advantage of high prices, selling pressure gradually increased, gradually moving downstream. The HSBC's posted rates were announced, with both the UK and the US flat, and the silver equalization tax was announced to have risen by 25. At this time, supply and demand were stable, and it hovered around 42 yuan. However, there was an eagerness among sellers, and it finally broke below the 40 yuan mark. Therefore, short sellers took advantage of the low prices to cover their positions. At noon, the trend was stable. The after-market gradually stabilized, and major players purchased actively. After the opening, it gradually recovered. However, because of the profit-taking at high prices, banks still supplied a lot. In the end, it was peaceful. The market conditions for today are recorded below.

The morning opening was 1,142.70 yuan, an increase of 2.40 yuan compared to the previous close. Chunyuan Yongda and Fayong Dingkang advanced to three yuan. Dadecheng, Hengchangyong, Fuxingyong, Chunyuan Yongyuan, Maoyong Dingkang Yingxiang sold off, falling to 1.30 yuan. The HSBC's posted rates were announced, with both the UK and the US flat. Dadecheng fluctuated, and the silver equalization tax rose by 25. At this time, it hovered around one yuan for quite a long time. Tongtaichang Hengyu Dadecheng Yuanfengyong Qiafengyong Qianchangxiang Yuanmaoyong Tongfu and others sold off, falling from two yuan to 39.70 yuan. Yuanmaoyong Fuxingyong Yuanchangyong Futaiheng Yuqingyong took advantage of the low prices to cover their positions, rising to 0.80 yuan. The afternoon close was 1,140.70 yuan.

The after-market opened at 1,140.90 yuan. Dafayong Yuanmaoyong covered their positions, rising to 1.10 yuan. Yuanmaoyong Yuanchangyong Daheng Yuanfengyong Dadecheng purchased positions, so Dadecheng Fuxingyong, although selling at 0.60 yuan, soon recovered to 1.80 yuan. Fuchunyong Qiafengyong Honglilai advanced, rising to 1.80 yuan. Futaiheng Yuanmaoyong still sold off at high prices, and the closing retreated to 1,141 yuan. The market was slightly weak after the close.

The settlement price, based on the Central Bank's standard call loan price, was posted higher at 1,133 yuan, approximately 8 yuan higher than the closing price, and 4 yuan less than the previous close. The registration for this month is 1,137 yuan, and for July it is 1,141 yuan. The morning replenishment was 1,137 yuan, and pure gold was increased by 5 yuan to 1,147.70 yuan. The spot market conditions and forward trades were still quiet. Tianjin goods were increased by 11 yuan, and smelted pure gold was increased by 10 yuan, but there were no sellers.

Trading within the market was normal. In summary, Chunyuan Yongdingkang Yuxin Xiang Huixiang Qianchangxiang Shunmao Tongheng, etc., were on the buying side. Qiafengyong Yuanmaoyong Tongtaichang Hengchangyong Hongkang Yongxin Dayong Shunli, etc., were on the selling side. Xianghe Futaiyong Fuxingyong advanced and retreated, and Xiangfeng Dadecheng, etc., retreated and advanced.

Checking the day's market conditions, it shifted from stable to weak. The morning opening was 1,142.70 yuan, and the after-market close was 1,141 yuan. The highest price was 1,143 yuan, and the lowest price was 1,139.70 yuan, with a fluctuation of 3.30 yuan. As a result, it rose slightly by 0.70 yuan compared to the previous close. Securities - The Political Situation Controls the Bond Market 214

The Selling Pressure Grows Stronger - Market Prices Plunge by More Than One Yuan

Yesterday's market conditions at the Chinese Securities Exchange were due to rumors in the Southwest, which have been clearly published in various newspapers. Rumors from Hunan Province followed, and the selling pressure from various groups became increasingly strong. The long positions' defenses showed signs of wavering. With rumors intertwined, can this crisis be resolved on the eve of this critical moment of fortune and misfortune? It is not only the public debt market that is greatly affected. According to the trend, there is a possibility of continued decline. However, if the selling pressure on the surface eases slightly, a recovery is also easy. However, the overall trend should still depend on the political situation for a turnaround.
